Scattered Battles on the East African Front, Italian and Abyssinian Armies Consolidate Positions, Italian Army on the Northern Route Attacks Magal Without Success, Rome Official Report Southern Army Occupies Two Important Passes

(Rome) Today's official report stated that fighting broke out in the Danaleh defense zone on the southern front in Abyssinia. The Italian side suffered 14 Italian soldiers and 10 native soldiers killed and the opposing side suffered 50 killed and many wounded. (Reuters dispatch, 20th)

Asmara According to detailed reports received here today on the fighting on the southern front, the Italian army has seized the strategically important locations of Solaf and Gajiuli. The Abyssinian army there suffered heavy losses due to bombing by Italian aircraft. Five Italian aircraft were hit by gunfire but all returned safely to base. It is heard that this victory will demoralize the Abyssinian army. (Reuters dispatch, 20th)

(Rome) The Italian army on the southern route, attacking Abyssinia, has already occupied the area of Hilaf north of the city of Gelokubi. Military figures here believe that this move will make it easier for General Graziani, commander-in-chief of the southern route, to advance on the town of Gorahei (an important town in the Ogaden region), which is extremely important strategically. The Abyssinian forces are currently concentrating at Gorahei Town, with two routes: one led by General Nazibi, heading from Harar City along the Fafan River to Gorahei Town; the other led by General Destu, the Abyssinian son-in-law, heading from the southwest along the Wabi Shebelle River to the town. The Italian military strategy is to surround the Abyssinian forces in Gorahei Town, forcing them to retreat north to Harar City. (Havas dispatch, 21st)

Addis Ababa Fighting on the southern front is still quiet. Abyssinian forces are currently constructing solid defensive works in Dagapo to prevent Italian forces from invading Harar. Dagapo is 120 miles southeast of Harar. It is heard that the Abyssinian forces in Harar and Jijiga are currently suffering from spotted fever, and the British Somaliland of Lumberbera is rushing medicine to help them. (Reuters dispatch, 20th)

Axum The Italian army's northern front, in the 40 miles between Axum and Adigrat, has gradually become consolidated, preparing for the first major offensive. Military authorities at the Italian headquarters today estimated that there are approximately 100,000 Abyssinian troops distributed in various locations within 100 miles in front of the Italian front. However, there is currently no fighting on the entire northern front. According to news here, the number of Italian casualties to date is one officer, five soldiers, and 23 Ascari soldiers. In addition, 70 soldiers were injured. At the same time, Italian aircraft are still bombing Abyssinian troop concentration points in various nearby locations. (National Electric, 20th)

Asmara From the look of things, the second major objective of the Italian army's northern advance, the city of Magal, 65 miles southeast of Aduwa, cannot be obtained without a major battle. Reconnaissance aircraft returning from the front claim that Abyssinian General Gaza is currently leading a large force from the southwest towards Magal, and another large force is guarding the previously occupied positions. At the same time, the Italian army is preparing to attack and is gradually occupying the mountains around Adigrat. The arrival of Italian Chief of Staff General Badoglio at the front has aroused various speculations. According to interviews with General and Reuters reporters, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini may visit the battlefield one day, which is also expected. Mussolini's large portraits are prominently displayed in the areas occupied by the Italian army, which is clear evidence that he can win the hearts of the people. (Reuters dispatch, 21st)

Italian Aircraft Carry Out Extensive Bombing, Progress on the Southern Front

(London) According to a telegram received here, the Italian army on the southern front killed many Abyssinian soldiers today. It is claimed that Italian aircraft bombed Abyssinian trenches in Dahelai and Hilaf, and used machine guns to strafe. Afterwards, Italian and Ascari soldiers charged forward. The Abyssinian army resisted strongly. After several hand-to-hand combats, the Italian army was able to occupy the position, but the first charge was repelled. (National Electric, 21st)

Tigray Front According to our correspondent Bal, the Italian army on the Somaliland front has made important progress and has occupied the Hilaf area north of the city of Gelokubi, capturing two cannons, multiple trucks, and countless prisoners. Hilaf is located midway between Gorahei Town (in the Ogaden region) and Italian Somaliland. Recently, the Abyssinian army was preparing to resist the Italian army's in-depth advance there, but it has now been occupied by the Italian army. Also, ten Italian aircraft flew to the town of Dahelai to carry out bombing and dropped incendiary bombs, causing fires. The Abyssinian army has recently deployed heavy troops along the Wabi Shebelle River in the Garafu area for defense. The aforementioned town of Dahelai, which was bombed, is not far from that position. In addition, Italian aircraft continue to bomb the Purtoni area along the Wabi Shebelle River. (Havas dispatch, 21st)

Two Columns Lose Contact in the Desert

Addis Ababa Our special correspondent Auchina reports the following military news from the front:

(1) "Eastern Front": Recently, two Italian columns have advanced from Mount Musayari. The first column advanced too quickly, resulting in getting lost in the hot desert area and losing contact with the second column carrying supplies. It had to be temporarily supplied with food and water by aircraft. In addition, road-building troops near Mount Musayari have contracted eye diseases due to the infection of germs from rotten wood used for road building. (2) "Northern Front" is currently in a state of stagnation. (3) "Southern Front": Rumors that the Italian army in the Ogaden area has occupied the Gelokubi water source, but the radio station there is still working as usual.

In short, the real fighting has not yet begun on all sides. The majority of the Abyssinian forces are concentrated in Tigray Province, because the climate, geographical conditions, and strong folk customs of that province are sufficient to temporarily hinder the Italian army's progress. (Havas dispatch, 20th)

Italian Army Wins Hearts and Minds, Local Chiefs Surrender

Aduwa Since Italian General Tai Bono, commander of the Italian army's northern route, ordered all Abyssinian clergy and soldiers who do not surrender to the Italian authorities within ten days to be regarded as enemies, 200 Cop脫派 monks and several lower-level chiefs have surrendered to the Italian army today. (National Electric, 21st)

(Rome) According to news from the city of Aksum in Abyssinia, more than 200 Cop脱派 churches in the area have jointly surrendered to the Italian army, including Maria, the son of the chief of the Echaha area. The majority of villagers in the Italian-occupied areas have turned in their privately owned rifles manufactured by European factories to the Italian army. The abolition of slavery by General Tai Bono, High Commissioner for East Africa, has not caused unrest among the slave owners, because the existing slaves, although restored to freedom, can still serve as servants or soldiers in their masters' homes. In order to win the hearts and minds of the people, the Italian army is implementing various benevolent acts to avoid causing ill will among the Abyssinian people. For example, after the Italian army occupied the city of Aksum, it distributed the wheat stored by the Abyssinian authorities in the city to nearby residents. At the same time, it is expanding sanitation facilities in the occupied areas and establishing many temporary aid stations. In addition, it plans to establish several hospitals and hire doctors with colonial medical experience to serve the natives. The first hospital will be established in the city of Aduwa and is currently being set up and should be completed soon. (Havas dispatch, 21st)

阿國各地戰士　開赴前綫作戰

From Aking: Warriors from all parts of Abyssinia continue to arrive in the capital. After being equipped with weapons and ammunition by the authorities, they are being dispatched to the front lines for combat. As for the destinations and operational plans, due to military secrets, nothing has been disclosed. General Yabaaba's warriors from the Gofa region also arrived here this morning and are stationed 20 kilometers outside the capital. All the bullets they carried were carefully inspected by the Abyssinian Imperial Guard because, a few days ago, many troops coming from the interior were found to be carrying dumdum bullets. Since the International Red Cross Convention prohibits the use of dumdum bullets, the Abyssinian Emperor has specifically prohibited his subordinates from carrying this type of bullet. However, it is rumored that Italian troops are still using dumdum bullets in combat, but this has not been confirmed. It is still unknown whether the Abyssinian Emperor is preparing to lodge a formal protest with the Geneva authorities regarding this matter. Furthermore, the Abyssinian Emperor's front lines recently captured a large number of Italian spies, who will soon be brought to the capital for separate interrogation. (20th Muharram dispatch)

意軍衛生狀況　據稱甚形良好

From Massawa: According to authorities, since the Italian army started the war in Abyssinia on October 3rd, a total of 233 soldiers have fallen ill, with only three fatalities. Since October 2nd, 212 Italian soldiers in Eritrea have returned home due to illness, mostly suffering from fevers. The Italian army has built 183 miles of new roads and dug 121 wells in the occupied territories of Abyssinia. Merchants are now following the army closely. Italians and Eritreans have already opened many shops in Adigrat and Hintalo. Sir Gastellani, a famous doctor in charge of sanitation in the occupied territories of Abyssinia, is very satisfied with the health of the Italian troops, saying that the sanitation of the Italian troops on the northern front is very good. Only one hospital ship carried sick soldiers back to Italy last month, totaling 202 officers and soldiers, with no wounded. There are now five ships converted into hospital ships, one of which is permanently stationed in Massawa. (October 20th Reuters dispatch)

法參院改選結果　左派勢力加增　賴伐爾獲選政府地位益固　共黨佔有席位此爲第一次

(Paris) Premier Laval's mediation for peace is now deeply popular, allowing him to win today's Senate election. Laval has now been re-elected. However, the Zena district is extremely left-leaning, and the other nine candidates who received the same number of votes as Laval have all lost. It was learned today that Laval believes this election result is due to the support he has gained for his policies on the Italo-Abyssinian conflict and European issues. (October 20th National Dispatch)

(Paris) One-third of the French Senate has been re-elected. The highlight is the election of the current Premier and Foreign Minister Laval, which has further consolidated the position of the French government. Although there was active and significant opposition from the left wing, Laval ultimately won. His domestic and foreign policies have gained the trust of the people. Efforts by left-wing parties in the parliament to overthrow the government in the future may not succeed. Mr. Basile has been elected in the Seine Province, making him the first Communist Party member to join the French Senate. The final result of the election is that the current situation can be maintained, and the Radical Party remains one of the most influential parties. (October 30th Reuters dispatch)

(Paris) Today's senatorial election involved re-electing one-third of the senators, with two rounds of voting. A total of 107 senators were elected. The number of seats obtained by each party is shown in the following table:

Non-affiliated 2 seats, Conservative Party 1 seat, Republican Party 26 seats, Left Republican Party 17 seats, Non-affiliated Radical Party 5 seats, Radical Socialist Party 38 seats, Non-affiliated Socialist Party 2 seats, New Socialist Party 4 seats, Socialist Party (i.e., the French branch of the Second International) 10 seats, Communist Party 2 seats, totaling 107 seats.

Although the results of this re-election do not significantly change the distribution of power among the parties in the Senate, the strength of the left wing has increased. In total, among the 107 seats elected, the right-wing and central parties account for 51 seats, while the left-wing and extreme left-wing parties account for 56 seats. This is the first time that the Communist Party has been elected to the Senate. The party leader, Xiang, is also among those elected. It is noted that the Senate election adopts a restricted election system. A portion of the electors are representatives of municipal councils. Since the recent municipal council elections, the left-wing parties have won victories. Generally, it was expected that the United Front of the left wing would win in the Senate re-election, and this has now happened, especially in the Seine Province, which includes the districts of Paris. After the first round of voting, the United Front of the left wing immediately elected seven people. (October 21st Havas dispatch)

北海狂風怒號　船隻擱淺遇險

(London) At the end of the week, gales raged across the Atlantic, the North Sea, and the English Channel, causing significant damage to ships. Five people died and many were injured throughout England. The Glasgow steamship "Fotoria" sank 700 miles off the coast of Ireland, and the lives of those on board are feared to be in danger. Thirty-seven sailors escaped in several small boats, but despite being searched for by several ships for 24 hours, they have not been found. A Newcastle coal ship also capsized in the storm. Fortunately, all 22 crew members were rescued by a Norwegian ship. The German ship "Olfort" was initially reported to have lost its thruster, and there has been no news since. There were a total of 25 people on board. The French ship "Agral" ran aground on a beach near Westdie. The sailors are still staying on board. (October 21st Reuters dispatch)

Amsterdam: A hurricane occurred in the North Sea today. The British freighter "Ben Dennis" has capsized, but all 23 sailors on board were rescued by the Norwegian ship "Alyeska". The "Ben Dennis" had a tonnage of approximately 2,000 tons. It was also learned here that the French freighter "Atra", weighing 5,872 tons, ran aground on Anlem Island. The German battleship "Heel" is parked nearby to provide assistance if necessary. Four other ships sent out distress signals today. The four ships are the Italian freighter "Birna", the French freighter "Olfana" weighing 2,114 tons, the "Gadava" sailing between Latvia and Belgium weighing 1,900 tons, and the freighter "Ladic", of unknown nationality. The Dutch Lauter Company mail ship "Iford," which was reported to be in distress yesterday, sent a wireless message today stating that the ship had narrowly avoided running aground. (October 20th National Dispatch)

希臘復辟運動　現總理力主恢復王泉

Athens: Prime Minister Gondyles recently gave an interview to a reporter from the "Kadirini News," stating, "The nation's politics should now be thoroughly reformed. The basic points of reform are threefold: (1) Restore the monarchy and consolidate royal power, so that the King becomes the supreme arbiter of all parties; (2) Reform the administrative organs; (3) Increase administrative power. However, in order to implement this platform, it must be approved by the King. Therefore, after the King returns to the country and is restored to his position, the cabinet should submit its resignation." (October 20th Havas dispatch)

Athens: A military-civilian carnival was held at the Athens stadium today. Government officials attended, and the crowd shouted "Long live King George II of Greece!" Furthermore, according to the Athens News Agency, rallies were also held in four cities in the provinces today. During the rally in Thessaloniki, former Prime Minister Tsaldaris gave a speech to the crowd, also advocating for inviting George II to return to the country and be restored to his position. (October 20th Havas dispatch)

Athens: The royalists recently held a large rally at the stadium, with approximately 60,000 participants. Regent Gondyles attended the rally and gave a speech, stating, "Although the new government includes several important leaders of the People's Party, the government has no intention of adopting new party politics. On the contrary, we should eliminate party strife and enable the national government to achieve its purely patriotic goals. Furthermore, the National Assembly will vote to abolish the republican system, while ensuring that all voters participating in the plebiscite are in an equal position. The National Assembly fully respects the sovereignty of the people, allowing the people to make the final decision on the issue of the form of government. At present, the vast majority of the people hope to achieve restoration, and since the abolition of the republican system, the general calls for a republic have ceased, and the country has returned to peace." (October 21st Havas dispatch)

漢德森逝世

(London) Henderson, Chairman of the League of Nations Disarmament Conference, passed away today. It is unknown how strongly Italy's attack on Abyssinia has affected Britain. Henderson's attending physician was well aware of his deep concern for the European situation, so since the start of the war, he has prohibited him from reading newspapers and told visitors not to mention the Italo-Abyssinian war to him. Henderson's death is a great loss to the millions of British workers whom he has led for many years. Even leading figures in politics have praised his achievements. Sir Chamberlain, who served in the wartime cabinet with Henderson, stated that everyone admired Henderson's dedication to peace. Viscount Cecil, a champion of peace, stated that Henderson's death is a cause for mourning for the future of peace. Atlee, the recently elected leader of the Labour Party, stated that no one could match Henderson's dedication to public service and commitment to peace. (October 20th National Dispatch)

(London) Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference and former British Foreign Secretary, one of the most prominent figures in the British Labour movement, passed away today at the age of 72. He was born on September 13, 1863. He learned the casting trade as a child. He was a trade union official and was elected as a Member of Parliament in 1903, serving for more than 30 years. In 1917, he joined the wartime cabinet as a minister without portfolio. In 1924, he served as the Home Secretary in the Labour government. From 1929 to 1931, he served as Foreign Secretary, deeply trusted by the then Prime Minister MacDonald. When MacDonald reorganized the national unity government, Henderson and other Labour leaders were dissatisfied with MacDonald's actions and resigned in anger. When he was in charge of foreign affairs, the Disarmament Conference elected him as its chairman. Although he later left the British government, he was unwilling to give up his position as chairman of the Disarmament Conference. It is almost unprecedented for a politician in opposition to chair such an important international conference. (October 20th Reuters dispatch)

Portrait of Mr. Henderson

美著名探險家　葛雷萊將軍逝世　曾著有北極探隊記一書

(Washington) General A.W. Greely, a famous American military figure, explorer, and author, has passed away at the age of 91. He served in the military since the outbreak of the Civil War, serving the country for 50 years. In 1881, he led an expedition into the Arctic region with 25 people. Only seven survived, including Greely. Although the sacrifice was great, the world learned that there were thousands of miles of land in the Arctic region. The American Geographical Society awarded him a medal, and the American government promoted him in the military, commending his achievements. Greely wrote many books on the climate conditions in various parts of the world, and his Arctic Exploration Account was particularly popular. At the age of eighty, he wrote another book entitled "The Arctic Region in the Twentieth Century," published in 1928. Greely paid close attention to science and made many contributions to American radio and aviation. (October 20th Reuters dispatch)

墨西哥　亂事未炍平

Nogales, Mexico: Sporadic warfare in Mexico will now inevitably be prolonged. The rebels of Sonora, assisted by the central government's cavalry and air force, have retreated to the source of the uprising, holding the dangerous terrain of the suburbs. It has been learned here that the Governor of Sonora Province, Ramos, submitted his resignation in Mexico on Saturday. His successor will be announced within 48 hours. (October 20th National Dispatch)

十月二十一日路透社特約商情電

October 21st Reuters Special Commercial Dispatch

Gold and Silver

British Gold: The London gold price today was 141 shillings and 5 pence, falling by 2.5 pence.

British Silver: The London silver market was stable today, with no price movement. Spot and futures were both 29 pence and 3225. The United States bought, and India and China sold.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The opening exchange rate for British pounds to US dollars was $4.91875, the same as the closing rate on Saturday. It fell by 4375 at noon, and then rose by 375 at 2:00 PM to $4.918125.

British-French: The opening price was 74 francs and 62, an increase of six pounds. It fell by eight pounds at noon, and then rose by three pounds at 1:00 PM to 74 francs and 57. There were no changes afterward.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: All sell-offs were absorbed when the New York cotton market opened. Prices rose by 3-5 pounds. Trading was not active. The market was sluggish during power outages.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market turned loose today. At 1:00 PM, the January futures price was 6.035, a decrease of six pounds.

British Wheat: Although there were unfavorable foreign dispatches this morning, the Liverpool wheat market was stable. At 1:00 PM, the December futures price remained at 6 shillings and 5.5 pence, unchanged.

American Wheat: Although there was discouraging news from South America and Australia, the Chicago wheat market opened high at 125, but trading was slow. Grains opened up 25, but there was very little trading and no price movement.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market was quiet this morning. The January-March futures opened at 6 pence and 4375, the same as the closing price on Saturday. There was no price change at noon.

New York: News that the export tax on native rubber from the Dutch East Indies has increased again has improved the New York rubber market. Prices are very stable. The opening price was up one pound. Prices continued to rise slightly before noon, but trading was limited.

Securities

New York: The New York securities market was very firm this morning. At the opening, except for a slight downward trend in mining stocks, the prices of various securities rose due to active buying. However, when prices were high, there was profit-taking, so prices fell slightly. The average price of the Dow Jones 30 industrial stocks opened at 173.57, an increase of 48 pounds. Former Japanese Ambassador to China, Shigemitsu, Hosts Economic Survey Mission

Deep rapport between financial circles of both countries; plan to establish an organization to promote bilateral trade

Tokyo Dispatch: The economic survey mission, since arriving in Tokyo a week ago, has been extremely busy with daily receptions, banquets, tours, and symposiums. By the 14th, discussions on trade between the two countries had generally come to a conclusion. The key to improving relations between the two countries lies in mutual economic benefit and assistance. The Japanese side also holds the same view. This time, financial leaders from both countries gathered to hold frank discussions, resulting in a very harmonious rapport. A unanimous agreement was reached to jointly initiate an organization to promote trade between the two countries by figures from the financial sectors of both sides. After the completion of the economic discussions, on the 14th, Foreign Vice-Minister Shigemitsu hosted a luncheon at his residence, attended by various bureau chiefs. Shigemitsu delivered a speech, stating, "In recent years, Japan's industry has developed rapidly. We welcome the visit of leaders from the Chinese economic community and believe that it will be greatly beneficial to the future of both countries. Many of you are old friends of mine, and this is a rare opportunity. I am very honored by your presence today and hope to have a pleasant conversation." Wu Dingchang then gave a speech, stating in essence, "When Mr. Shigemitsu served as Ambassador to China, it was a time of diplomatic difficulty between China and Japan. We have long been aware of Mr. Shigemitsu's efforts for the happiness of relations between the two countries. The current difficulties in the Sino-Japanese situation have not only not diminished, but may have even intensified. Therefore, we cannot help but hope that Mr. Shigemitsu will exert even greater effort. At the tea party the other day, I heard Foreign Minister Hirota cite the saying from the Analects, 'If you don't receive commands, you will make wealth.’ I hope that both countries will pursue economic exchanges with benevolence and righteousness. Today, I will quote Mencius's reply to King Xuan of Qi's question, 'Is there a way to befriend neighboring countries?' Mencius replied, 'Yes. Only the benevolent can serve the small with the great, and only the wise can serve the great with the small.' I feel that Japan, since the Meiji Restoration, has been quite capable of utilizing this diplomatic principle. In the past, it can be said that it has exhausted the abilities of the wise. The most prominent example is the Anglo-Japanese Alliance, which achieved the greatest diplomatic success. Now that Japan's national strength is increasing day by day, it has reached the point where it should study how to serve the small with the great. However, serving the small with the great is more difficult than serving the great with the small, because it is often easy to interpret serving the small as subjugating the small, which violates the clear instruction in the Four Books that 'those who subdue people with force do not win their hearts.' Therefore, I hope that Japan can understand the principle of serving the small with the great. In the future of Sino-Japanese diplomacy, it will surely achieve the greatest success." Afterwards, they engaged in casual conversation, and the gathering ended happily around 2 PM. At 3 PM, they went to the private residence of Fujiyama, president of Dai-Nippon Sugar Manufacturing Co., Ltd., to attend a tea party. At 9 PM, they took the night train from Tokyo to Osaka for a tour. They are scheduled to return to Tokyo in a week and then disband and return to their respective countries.

The Sugar Cane Industry in Chaozhou and Shantou

The Monopoly Bureau cracks down on private sales

Shantou Dispatch: The Chaozhou-Shantou First Sugar Factory, this spring, selected a factory site in Quxi, Jieyang, and purchased more than 50 mu of private land, of which seventy to eighty percent has been completed. Most of the main machinery has been installed. The Quxi location has very convenient water and land transportation. Sugar production can begin next month. According to Zheng Zonghan, a member of the factory's preparatory committee, the purchase of sugarcane from the people has been entrusted to the Huasheng Company. The price is set at 7 hao per dan (100 jin). The Huasheng Company has ordered 9.8 million dan from Jieyang, Puning, and Chaoan counties, which can be continuously supplied to the factory for manufacturing. Currently, sugarcane farmers in the Chaozhou and Jieyang rural areas are very worried about the sugar factory purchasing sugarcane from the people because: (1) The government stipulates 7 hao per dan of sugarcane, and the handling Huasheng Company also wants to earn a commission of 1 hao and several fen; (2) For sugarcane fields far from Quxi, manual carrying and transportation by boats will add another 1 hao and several fen of costs per dan; (3) If the sugarcane tails are also transported, there will be a lack of sugarcane seeds for next year. If the sugarcane tails are cut off, the farmers will suffer too much loss; (4) Once the sugarcane is sold, the farmers' homes will lack fuel for cooking throughout the year; (5) If the sugarcane is cut and handed over too late, the sugar juice will be less, and the weight will also be lighter, resulting in too much loss; (6) The sugarcane in the field must wait for the factory's orders, and if it is left in the field for too long, it will delay spring plowing. Furthermore, the fertilizer and bean cakes used for planting sugarcane this year have already increased in price, and the land rent has also been changed to land tax. The sugarcane sold, after deducting the handling fees and transportation fees by the handlers, will only yield 4 or 5 hao, which is not even enough to offset the fertilizer and land rent. Therefore, the farmers are all very disappointed.

The Chaozhou-Shantou Provincial Sugar Monopoly Bureau has a public warehouse in Shantou. White sugar is transported from Guangzhou, and 6,000 to 7,000 dan can be sold in Chaozhou and Meizhou counties each month. The price is 17.5 yuan per dan. Each county has distribution points, and inspection teams and sugar inspectors are stationed at key transportation points. Boats, vehicles, households, and shops can be searched everywhere. Shops without permits cannot sell white sugar. Sugar sales permits must be renewed once a year. At the end of September, all permits will expire and new permits will be issued. In more than ten counties in Chaozhou and Meizhou, only 100 wholesale and retail business permits are issued for each market town and village. Those without this permit cannot engage in the sale and transportation of white sugar. In addition, 500 small retail business permits are issued. Shops that do not display this permit at the entrance cannot sell or store sugar in the store. These measures can be said to be extremely thorough.

The Chaozhou area was originally a region that produced native sugar. The annual export of native sugar is no less than 2 to 3 million dan. Native sugar merchants occupy an important position in the economic and commercial sectors. Since the provincial government implemented a white sugar monopoly, restrictions and management have been added to native sugar. The previously promulgated measures for registering native sugar were not understood and sympathized by the masses in Chaozhou and Shantou, so they were improved. After native sugar is registered, those who transport it out of the province must obtain a transportation and sales permit from the provincial sugarcane transportation and sales branch office at the place of origin or transit, in order to transfer it. If it arrives in Shantou, the permit must be taken to the Shantou branch office to cancel the number before it can be exported. If it is transported and sold within the province, and the place of arrival does not have a transportation and sales branch office, the transportation and sales permit will be mailed back to the place where the transportation and sales permit was originally issued to cancel the number. The government's reason for taking these procedures of checking, registering, obtaining transportation permits, release forms, and canceling numbers everywhere is said to be to prevent the mixing of foreign sugar, to prevent the development of native sugar, and to avoid affecting the progress of sugar production and sugarcane purchases.

Anhui Province: Conscripting Labor for Water Conservancy Projects; Regulations for Conscripting Labor in Various Counties Have Been Drafted

Anqing Dispatch: The Anhui Construction Department believes that this year's water conservancy construction is about to enter the implementation and construction period. Regarding the organization and conscription of labor, a plan must be drafted. Therefore, the revised regulations for the Engineering Committee of each county and the newly drafted regulations for the conscription of labor for water conservancy in each county were submitted to the provincial government's regular meeting on the 18th and passed. The following is a transcript:

Regulations for Conscripting Labor for Water Conservancy in Various Counties

Article 1: In order to carry out water conservancy projects and conscript labor in various counties of this province, unless otherwise stipulated by laws and regulations, these regulations shall be followed. Article 2: Conscripted labor is divided into two types: obligatory labor and beneficiary labor. Those who are required to perform labor services under laws and regulations are obligatory labor, and those who benefit from a certain water conservancy project are beneficiary labor. Article 3: The conscription period is based on the principle of agricultural slack season, but this does not apply to special emergency projects. Article 4: Workers subject to conscription must provide their own meals, lodging, and tools. Article 5: People in the province aged 18 to 50 shall be subject to obligatory labor, serving three to seven days each year. Article 6: Government employees and military officers and soldiers shall participate in local labor services. Article 7: Faculty and students of schools above the middle school level shall each serve ten days of labor service during the annual vacation and winter vacation. Article 8: Obligatory labor shall not be exempted unless one of the following reasons exists: (1) They have already been conscripted as beneficiary labor for a certain water conservancy project; (2) They have already been conscripted for road construction, material production, or other labor services; (3) They have special reasons that have been verified and confirmed. Article 9: Beneficiary labor shall be allocated based on the specific project conditions, the benefited farmland, industry, commerce, navigation, and benefited households, in order to complete the project as the standard. Article 10: Before the implementation of the work schedule, a conscription roster shall be prepared, and work sections shall be allocated according to the plan, specifying the date and notifying each worker to arrive on time. Article 11: After the workers are conscripted, they shall be organized uniformly and checked daily. Article 12: If a worker subject to conscription cannot come in person and no one can replace him, he may pay a substitute fee based on the above number. The amount to be paid for each worker shall be stipulated and announced by the county government in advance. Article 13: The county government shall immediately hire a substitute worker with the substitute fee collected and announce the names of the original conscripted person and the substitute worker at the same time. Article 14: Detailed rules for the implementation of conscription shall be formulated by each county in consideration of local conditions and reported to the provincial government for record. Article 15: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time. Article 16: These regulations shall come into effect from the date of promulgation.

Regulations for the Water Conservancy Engineering Committee of Each County

Article 1: This committee is established for the purpose of preventing floods and managing water conservancy. A Water Conservancy Engineering Committee shall be established in the County Government Bureau in each county, and a Water Conservancy Engineering Committee branch shall be established in each district office. Article 2: The committee shall have nine to eleven members. The county magistrate, the head of the relevant County Government section, and the chairman of the Financial Committee shall be ex officio members. The remaining members shall be selected by the county magistrate from among the local gentry familiar with water conservancy and appointed. The county magistrate shall be the chairman of the committee, and the county magistrate shall appoint one of the members as the vice-chairman. Article 3: Each branch shall have seven to nine members. The district chief shall be an ex officio member. The remaining members shall be selected by the county magistrate from among the local gentry of the district and appointed. The district chief shall be the chairman of the committee, and the county magistrate shall appoint one of the members as the vice-chairman. Article 4: The committee and branches may hire local gentry who are familiar with water conservancy and enthusiastic about public welfare as consultants. Article 5: The committee and branches shall handle affairs in groups as follows: Group A: General Affairs Group: 1. Matters related to meetings; 2. Matters related to the collection, safekeeping, receipt, expenditure, and audit of construction funds; 3. Top budget calculation, final account preparation matters; 4. Matters related to the preparation, receipt, dispatch, and safekeeping of documents; 5. Other matters not belonging to the engineering group. Group B: Engineering Group: 1. Matters related to engineering investigation and survey; 2. Matters related to engineering guidance and supervision; 3. Matters related to the conscription, checking, and management of workers; 4. Matters related to engineering reports; 5. Other engineering matters. Article 6: Each group of the committee and branches shall have one director, who shall be appointed by the chairman of the committee. Article 7: The chairman, vice-chairman, and group directors shall be stationed at the meeting at all times. Article 8: The Standing Committee of the Committee shall meet once a month. Temporary meetings shall be convened by the Chairman of the Committee. Members shall not be absent from meetings unless there are special circumstances. Consultants and group directors may attend meetings. Article 9: Water conservancy projects to be carried out in each county shall be planned by the committee convening a joint meeting of representatives of the branches before the start of the year, and submitted to the county government for submission to the provincial government for approval. Article 10: The affairs of the committee and branches shall be handled by the staff of the county government and district office respectively. If necessary, employees may be hired at discretion. Article 11: Members shall be volunteer positions. Group directors and employees may be paid salaries and allowances at discretion. Article 12: The necessary office expenses and supervision expenses of the committee and branches shall be budgeted, together with the fundraising methods, and submitted to the provincial government for approval by the County Government Bureau. Article 13: The committee's seal and the branch's seal shall be issued by the county government and the models shall be reported to the provincial government for record. Article 14: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time. Article 15: These regulations shall come into effect from the date of promulgation.

Songjiang: Construction Department Technician Inspects Branch Line

After the county government completed the construction of the Songsi Road, it continued in late September to start work on a branch line from the North Gate to the New East Gate to connect to Songwei Road. It passes through the prosperous streets of the East Gate and requires the demolition of more than 40 private houses, which does not match the three and a half rooms of the former Times Hall owned by Mr. Jin. This has led to merchants and local people in the East Gate requesting assistance and almost causing disputes. The county government temporarily ordered the suspension of work and telegraphed the Construction Department to send personnel to inspect. The Construction Department specially appointed Mr. Yang Tingzuo, a technician, who arrived in Songjiang on the 21st. After visiting County Magistrate Li, he went with him to the branch line for a field inspection and invited local people Qian Xuanqing, Zhu Jwang, Yao Lianbo, etc., as well as the County Party Department of the Koumintang, the County Chamber of Commerce, and Shen Fuyun, the head of the First District, to talk at the county government. Technician Wu was very dissatisfied with the discrepancy in the piers of the demolished houses reported by the competent department. However, regarding the change of line, because the base along the city is within six meters, the regulations do not allow any buildings, so there is no way to change the original line. Regarding the compensation for the demolition of houses for the victims, it was agreed to increase the compensation and revise the original budget. He asked those present to go out and explain tactfully, etc. Mr. Qian and others stated that the losses of the people were too heavy and asked for the prompt arrangement of cash payments to take care of the people's difficulties, etc. It was not until 6 PM that the meeting ended. Technician Wu took the car back to the province that night to report back.

Suzhou: Gang Robbery; Police and Bandits Exchange Fire

In the Tangjiahu area of Wujiang, more than 30 lake bandits arrived by boat on the evening of the 20th and landed to rob. This was learned by the local Public Security Branch, and Patrol Chief Peng led the police to suppress them, opening fire. The bandit leader also fired back, and the two sides held each other for three hours. As a result, the bandits were unable to resist and retreated. The police captured seven lake bandits, three bandit women, and four bandit boats. They were sent to the Wujiang Public Security Bureau on the 21st for interrogation.

Cupping Causes a Fatality

Yuan Hanwen, who specializes in broadcasting humorous songs on the Bailing Radio Station, has a thriving career of entertaining at gatherings every day due to his eloquent talent. He recently moved to No. 3, Shijia Alley. On the 20th, Ding Wanquan, a colleague from the Xinxingyuan Restaurant on nearby Linkan Road, suddenly suffered from acute cupping syndrome with severe abdominal pain. Accompanied by his colleague Xue Genquan, he was taken to Yuan's place to ask Yuan to perform cupping. However, as soon as the needle was inserted, Ding died on a rattan chair in Yuan's house. The police officer on duty immediately arrested Yuan. The deceased remained stiffly seated on Yuan's chair until 2 PM on the 21st. The viewers were constantly arriving and leaving, and the threshold was worn through. The police station sent police officers to take care of him. At about 3 PM, a prosecutor from the local court arrived to examine the body.

Wuxi: Yu Kang Yarn Factory Resumes Operations Yesterday

The Yu Kang Yarn Factory in Zhoushanbang previously announced the suspension of work due to the accumulation of inventory and poor business operations. The shareholders' meeting appointed Xue Huidong and four others to organize a reorganization committee to start the reorganization and elected Yang Guanchang as manager and Zhou Jimei and others as executive directors. Since March, the reorganization plan has been finalized. In terms of industrial affairs, there has been a thorough innovation, and textile engineer Du Chunzuo has been hired as the director of industrial affairs. It officially started work on the 21st, which is also a good sign for the future of Wuxi's industry.

Yangzhou: City and Township Second Fire Drill

The Second Fire Drill Competition in the City and Township of Jiangdu was held at 3 PM on the 20th at the Dajiao Field outside the West Gate. There were 26 public and private fire brigades, a total of 892 people, as well as County Magistrate Ma Zhenbang, all the police chiefs and police officers of the Public Security Bureau, and about 1,000 spectators. At about 3 PM, the opening ceremony was held. County Magistrate Ma presided over the meeting and led the ceremony. The chairman reported on the significance of the fire drill, and then the head of the Public Security Bureau, Zhang Shu, talked about the relationship between air defense and fire protection. After the ceremony, the team was inspected, and Yao Yuncong, the head of the First Section of the Public Security Bureau, was the commander-in-chief and reported the start of the inspection. County Magistrate Ma and others inspected the site in turn for a week, and then held a divisional parade. The entire team circled the field for a week, and then the equipment was inspected. "Divided the dragon to shoot high and far," the fire drill "divided into the departure fluid to save the fire road, save people and save things gathered," and the meeting ended at about 6 PM.

Haimen: Thorough Investigation of Illegal Collection of Exorbitant Taxes

The Niu Hong, Songji, Da'an, Qinglong, Lingdian, and other port areas of this county collect water and land police donations from passing travelers, as well as carrying force. The county people Yu Chanzhi and others requested the Jiangsu Provincial Donation and Tax Supervision Committee to send personnel to conduct a thorough investigation. The committee believes that the water and land police donations in various ports are exorbitant, disturbing the people, and the Department of Finance has long ordered them to be stopped. The carrying force has also been stipulated at 1.5 jiao per person and should not be requested extra. However, the ports and piers dared to collect them in violation of the order, which is illegal. The Department of Finance ordered the county government on the 18th to thoroughly investigate and punish them according to the law in order to avoid setting an example. The committee also believes that there are still illegal collections of the vehicle tax in Nantong, Haimen, and Qidong counties after the Department of Finance ordered the abolition. It has now sent investigator Shen Botao to Tonghai and Qidong counties to collect evidence for investigation.

Pinghu: Tax Police Seize 30,000 Jin of Smuggled Salt

The First District Brigade of the Zha Pu Tax Police learned on the 17th that salt smugglers in Si Dai were burning a large amount of smuggled salt and selling it outside the territory, so they secretly ordered their subordinates to go to various important roads to intercept them. On the 18th, they intercepted six smuggled salt boats at the Caishenmiao Bridge, three li south of the county seat. The smugglers did not resist and fled ashore. They immediately hired coolies to shake the boats to the team headquarters, counting more than 300 dans.

Three Female Servers Poisoned

The small taverns in this city have hired female servers for many years due to business relations. Recently, the Yuansheng Noodle Restaurant in front of the North Temple has also followed suit. On the 18th, Cui Laosong and Li Jingqing from Zhapu, and Wang Rongchun from this city, left the theater and agreed to have fun with the female servers (that is, to go to the female servers' place to drink). They went to the Yuansheng Restaurant to drink and chat. At first, they laughed and joked happily, but unexpectedly, at the end of the banquet, they felt unwell. Wang sent the two to the hotel and felt severe abdominal pain, unable to speak. Medical treatment was ineffective. On the 18th, Wang died. Cui and Li were still in danger.

Hangzhou: Willow Waves and Orioles Song is a New Park

The Hangzhou City Government previously designated the "Willow Waves and Orioles Song" area as a scenic residential area. Recently, it was ordered by the provincial government to plan and build a park in the area. Personnel were sent to investigate, taking the original road along the lake from Yongjinmen outside the lake entrance to the Qianwangtong statue as an example of being too close to the lake. The Huanhu Road in that area was ordered to be moved into the lake. It is planned to fill in a part of the land in the lake and develop it into a park. At the same time, the abandoned Huanhu Road line will be developed into a ten-foot-wide road, so that the park will be surrounded by roads in the future. Before the currently stipulated Huanhu Road is built, the lake transportation will also be connected. The high ground around the Qianwang Temple in Piyi can be reserved for building a park, but because the "Willow Waves and Orioles Song" base is only 1.8 mu, the land near the high ground is all private property. It is difficult to include it in the park. Therefore, it is planned to plant flowers and trees on the high ground of the Qianwang Temple and combine it with the "Willow Waves and Orioles Song" for consolidation. Adding the newly filled lake land mentioned above, there will be an area of more than eight mu, which is enough to develop a public area as a public tourist attraction in the Nanshan Road area. It is heard that Hangzhou City has made a plan based on this investigation report and submitted it to the provincial government, and first started to build roads and level the ground.

Jiaxing: Kidnapped Victim Escapes Bandit Boat in Nanhui

At about 6 PM on the 20th, the First Police Station of Tanghui Street, Jiaxing, suddenly received a report from a man with disheveled hair and short clothes, saying that he was Xu Weiqing, a 32-year-old surgeon from Nanhui County near Shanghai. On May 20th of the lunar calendar, he was kidnapped under the pretext of being invited to see a boil. For more than four months, he lived on a bandit boat. The bandits forced him to write a letter to his family, asking for a ransom of 20,000 yuan. Today, the boat was docked on the side of the Daqiao Bridge in Tanghe. Because two bandits who usually carried guns were going ashore to buy things, and the two bandits watching the victim were also asleep, he took the opportunity to go ashore and escape, following the road to this place, etc. The police station immediately reported to the police brigade by telephone to pursue and arrest the bandits in the Baibao Bridge area of Wangjiangjing Tang, but the bandit boat was not found. That night, the kidnapped victim was sent to the First Public Security Bureau for lodging. It was learned that the kidnapped victim's family still has an elderly mother, wife, three daughters, and one son. Director He of the Public Security Bureau has notified his family by telephone, ordering them to come to He County to pick up the kidnapped victim and reunite.

Xinghua: County Government Gazette Expense Allocation

The county government of this county recently issued a general order to the district offices, stating that the 83rd administrative meeting resolved to create a county government gazette to increase administrative efficiency. The required expenses are shared by the county government, the Education and Youth Bureau, various schools, the Anti-Smoking Association, the Real Estate Management Office, various district offices, the Security Team Headquarters, and the Public Security Bureau, etc. The allocation method is as follows: each township government shall also bear five cents per month, which shall be collected and remitted by the district office.

US Army Secretary Dern Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon, Attends Tea Party Hosted by US Consul General and Dinner Hosted by Minister Kong, Scheduled to Go to Nanjing Tonight and Take the Original Ship to the US on the 25th

US Vice President Garner and Secretary of War George H. Dern, having attended the Philippine Independence Government Establishment Ceremony, have already departed from the United States. Vice President Garner is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on November 2nd, while Secretary Dern arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 2:15 PM aboard the USS Chester. He is scheduled to go to Nanjing on the 24th to visit our authorities and will take the original ship to the Philippines on the morning of the 25th. The details are as follows:

Various Parties Welcome

Secretary Dern, accompanied by his wife, son, Colonel Hodges, Major Bishop, and others, a total of six people, departed from the United States on the 20th of last month aboard the USS Chester. After arriving in Japan, they arrived in China and entered the Wusongkou at 6:15 AM yesterday morning and berthed in the Yangshupu River at 7:00 AM. Minister of Military Affairs He Yingqin, represented by Xu Jinyuan, Mayor of Shanghai Wu Tiecheng, represented by Yu Hongjun, Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Yu Ming, US Ambassador to China Johnson, Commercial Counselor Arnold, Consul General to Shanghai Cunningham, Commander of the US Far East Fleet Admiral Yabaiheng, Commander of Shanghai Colonel Baimen, and others, all took the Jinghui special launch from the Bund wharf on Nanjing Road at 11:00 AM to welcome them. The US Army Command in Shanghai also sent two platoons of armed soldiers and a small band to the wharf to welcome them. The police also temporarily dispatched police officers to the wharf to guard the area.

Minister Kong's Banquet

Secretary Dern was originally scheduled to land at 12:00 PM, but it was temporarily changed to 2:15 PM due to some matter. Therefore, the welcoming personnel gradually dispersed at 12:00 PM and reassembled at the wharf before 2:00 PM to welcome Secretary Dern. At 2:15 PM, Secretary Dern transferred to a small speedboat and arrived at the Bund Bronze Man Wharf. He disembarked amidst the sound of military music and went to the US Consulate General to rest briefly. Then, at 5:30 PM, he went to the Columbia Country Club to attend a grand welcome tea party hosted by the US Consulate General in Shanghai. The US Consulate General also invited leaders from various circles in China and abroad to accompany him. At 8:00 PM, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi hosted a banquet at his private residence on Xiai'en Road, and also invited representatives from all walks of life to accompany him. The guests and hosts happily dispersed around 10:00 PM.

Going to Nanjing Tonight

Secretary Dern is scheduled to go to the Municipal Government in the city center this morning to visit Mayor Wu Tiecheng for ordinary courtesies. At noon, he will speak at the American Youth Association. At 11:00 PM, accompanied by US Ambassador Johnson, he will go to Nanjing to pay a visit to our authorities. He plans to stay in Nanjing for two days to visit various construction projects in the capital. He is scheduled to leave Nanjing by overnight express train on the evening of the 24th to return to Shanghai and take the original ship to the Philippines on the morning of the 25th to attend the Philippine Independence Government Establishment Ceremony. He will stay in the Philippines for two weeks and then return to the country via Shanghai and Japan.

Secretary Dern's Speech

Secretary Dern is 55 years old, and his wife is younger. Secretary Dern is tall and robust, full of energy, and approachable when talking to people. Yesterday, he wore a black formal dress. According to what he told reporters from various newspapers upon arriving in Shanghai, his trip to the Philippines was purely to attend the Philippine Independence Government Establishment Ceremony and had no other mission. He took the opportunity to visit everything in your country. When he passed through Japan, he also took the opportunity to visit briefly. When he returns to the country in the future, he will still follow the original route. If time permits at that time, he may stay longer. Secretary Dern continued, saying that the United States and China are two major countries in the Pacific, and the Philippines is an emerging country. The relationship between the three is extremely close, and it will definitely become closer in the future.

Foreign Media Reports

The ship berthed at the thirteenth and fourteenth buoys downstream of the Huangpu River after 9:00 AM. Before landing, Secretary Dern met with representatives of the Greater Shanghai Evening News in the ship's office. Secretary Dern was amiable and willing to have informal talks with ordinary people. He said that he was very happy to come to China. His visit to China did not carry any mission. His only mission abroad was to represent the US President at the establishment ceremony of the new Republic of the Philippines. He was very happy to take this opportunity to spend this very short time in the East. This was his first time to the East, and like others, he was full of curiosity and eager to visit China and Japan. We stayed in Honolulu for five days, followed by Yokohama for four days. He visited the Emperor in Tokyo and was entertained by the Minister of War, and had the opportunity to meet with various dignitaries. He also visited Nikko. He was particularly interested in Japanese rural life and the field scenery along the way. This time passing through China, he did not have the opportunity to see everything, but seeing the magnificence of the river view was enough to make people linger. Secretary Dern plans to go to Nanjing tomorrow night, and will be invited to a banquet by the President of the Executive Yuan on Wednesday evening, and will return to Shanghai on Thursday. He will attend Mayor Wu's banquet in the evening, and will take the original ship to the Philippines at 11:00 AM on Friday morning. The procedures for entertaining Chinese and foreign officials and gentry are as follows: At 5:30 PM on Monday afternoon, a welcome reception will be hosted by the American community at the American Country Club. Each guest will pay one yuan. At 8:00 PM, Minister Kong and his wife will host a banquet at their residence. From 6:00 PM to 8:00 PM, the officers of the Fourth Marine Regiment will host a welcome reception. At 8:15 PM, the US Consul General will host a banquet. At 11:00 PM in the afternoon, he will take a train to Nanjing. He will arrive in Nanjing on Wednesday. At 4:00 PM in the afternoon, he will visit the President of the Executive Yuan and will be invited to a banquet by the President in the evening. He will arrive in Shanghai at 7:00 AM on Thursday morning. At 7:20 PM, Mayor Wu will host a banquet. At around 11:00 AM on Friday morning, he will leave Shanghai by the USS Chester cruiser.

US Military Advisor to the Philippines, MacArthur, Arrives in Shanghai, Media Mogul Howard Accompanies Him

Xinsheng News Agency reported that a large number of US government officials are successively going to the Philippines to participate in the grand ceremony of the establishment of its new government. In addition to Secretary of War Dern, who arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning, and Vice President Garner, who will pass through Shanghai on the 2nd of next month, General Douglas MacArthur, the former commander-in-chief of the US military, who is now assigned as a military advisor to the Philippine government, also arrived in Shanghai at 9:00 PM last night aboard the Dollar Line's President Hoover, accompanied by his 86-year-old mother and subordinates. Senior Japanese Officials in Shanghai No Longer Hold Meetings, Had Talks at the No. 63 Garden the Night Before

Xinsheng News Agency reported that the three meetings of consular officials, military attachés of the army and navy, centered on representatives dispatched to China by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of the Army, and the Ministry of the Navy, have ended. Except for the consular meeting, which ended on the 19th, the two meetings of military attachés of the army and navy also ended yesterday morning. The joint meeting of the highest-level officials of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of the Army, and the Ministry of the Navy stationed in China will no longer be held. Because Ambassador Arima held a banquet at the No. 63 Garden on Jiangwan Road at 7:00 PM the day before to welcome the representatives Okamura, Honda, and Morishima, as well as the military attachés and consuls of the army and navy, opinions were exchanged and frank discussions were held at the banquet, and there was no need to hold another meeting. The following are the details of what Bii Eiichi, the spokesperson of the embassy, told the reporter of Xinsheng News Agency.

Japanese Ambassador Arima Akira hosted a grand banquet at the No. 63 Garden on Jiangwan Road at 7:00 PM the night before to welcome the three representatives dispatched to China by the Ministry of the Army, the Ministry of the Navy, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to convey their intentions, and to entertain the military attachés and consuls of the army and navy from various places who came to Shanghai to attend various meetings. The Japanese Army Attaché Conference in China continued to be held in the living room of the Japanese Army Counselor's Office at No. 923 Wuding Road at 9:00 AM yesterday morning. The attendees were still the 12 people including Major General Okamura. Outside the door of No. 923, Japanese military police and public security detectives were densely stationed, and the security was extremely tight. The meeting did not end until 12:00 PM at noon. It continued to be held on the ship yesterday morning at 8:00 AM. Those who participated included 19 staff members of the Marine Corps and the Third Fleet. The meeting also ended around 12:00 PM.

Iwai Denies There is a New Policy

Regarding the holding of the above two meetings, the army attaché conference lasted for 12 hours, and the naval military attaché conference lasted for 6 hours. It can be imagined that the two meetings took a long time, discussed many issues, and the military attachés from various places reported in detail. However, according to Ishii Eiichi, the spokesperson of the embassy, the content of the two military attaché conferences was not as sensational as reported in the news. First Special Court Rules that Huai Xing Li's Rent Should Be Paid at 80% of the Original Amount, Judging the Situation Fairly

The case of the landlord Yuan Mao Company of Huai Xing Li on East Xihua Road in this city, and the tenants Lin Daozhi, Huang Jusen, Chen Xingxiang, Wang Xueming, Wang Yulin, and others, suing each other for rent payment, eviction, and rent reduction, has been judged by Judge Mo Runhua of the First Special District Local Court, and the rent is allowed to be paid at 80% of the original amount. The judgment has been delivered to both parties yesterday afternoon. The judgment of the court is recorded as follows: (Reasons) The fact that the defendants owed the plaintiff rent is undisputed. What should be investigated is whether the defendants' claim that the original rent should be reduced and collected is reasonable. It is clearly stipulated in Article 442 of the Civil Code that if the leased object is real estate, the parties may apply to the court to increase or decrease the rent due to the rise and fall of its value. The defendants claimed that the recent market decline and the sharp drop in land prices are undeniable facts. Although the Land Evaluation Register of the Engineering Bureau has not fallen, since the bankruptcy of the banking industry in the past six months has been mostly caused by the lack of attention to real estate. The real estate price in Shanghai today is very different from what it used to be, as everyone knows. Therefore, the defendant's request to reduce the rent cannot be considered unreasonable. Moreover, the rent of the houses to the left and right of the defendants' residence has been reduced, and the defendants have submitted rent receipts and other documentary evidence. The fact that the first defendant's rent was reduced early has also been proven by the witness Feng Guihe in court. Therefore, their claim should be recognized as legitimate. However, the defendants' request to reduce the original rent by 40% is too low, and the landlord's loss is also huge. The original amount should be paid for the rent in the year of 1934, which should be paid at the original amount of the previous year. Since January of this year, all should be paid at 80%. The defendants are ordered to pay the plaintiff the amounts shown in the main text. The plaintiff's request for overpayment and the defendants' remaining counterclaims should be dismissed. It is also found that the defendants temporarily stopped paying the rent because the rent reduction issue has not been resolved, and the rent has been deposited in the bank. Since each of them has submitted the passbook as evidence, it can be seen that they did not deliberately owe the rent, and the contract cannot be terminated and the house cannot be evicted. The plaintiff's eviction lawsuit should also be dismissed. Regarding the part of the rent owed, the plaintiff's agent has stated that he can provide a guarantee before the execution and apply for provisional execution. According to law, the court should determine a considerable amount of guarantee and announce that the provisional execution is allowed after the guarantee is provided. Based on the above conclusions, the plaintiff's lawsuit and the defendant's counterclaim are partially reasonable and partially unreasonable, and they should be approved or dismissed separately.

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association sent a letter to Philipp, acting director of the Public Concession Engineering Bureau, yesterday, saying, "According to a letter from Fukang Soy Sauce Garden at the intersection of Yangshupu Yangshou Road and Huasheng Road, 'The rent of our store has been reduced by 20% since February of last year, which has become a fact. The rent receipts are all there. What happened last year has passed and is not a problem. However, it seems that the extra payments that have already been paid for the spring, summer, and autumn seasons this year should be removed in the winter. The case is corresponded and requested to your bureau to order the donation office to check the established cases and handle them in accordance with the uniform standard for the sake of your honor."

The National Federation of Commerce Cables the Ministry of Finance: Stop Heavy Taxes on Saltpeter and Sulfur; The Fireworks Industry Greatly Affected, Impoverished People's Livelihoods Threatened; Swiftly Order the Wanzai Saltpeter and Sulfur Bureau to Levy Taxes According to Previous Regulations

The National Federation of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, stating, "We have recently received a cable from the Jiangxi Wanzai County Chamber of Commerce on the 30th, which roughly states: According to a cable from the Wanzai County Fireworks Industry Association, since the county has been plagued by bandits, the fireworks industry has stagnated and the economy has collapsed. The livelihood of the majority of the county's residents depends on firecracker handicraft. Therefore, the lightness of the saltpeter and sulfur tax rate greatly affects the livelihoods of impoverished people. Now, Director Wu Dingsong is taking over the Wanzai saltpeter and sulfur tax collection, increasing the tax rate to six yuan per hundred catties of saltpeter and four yuan per hundred catties of sulfur, which can be described as exorbitant taxes. Furthermore, the business license tax is also being increased as before, forcing them to obtain licenses, causing various fireworks factories to be unable to bear the burden and now completely shutting down. If this is not stopped, not only will the firecracker industry be devastated, but the rural economy will also be greatly affected. In the past, Wanzai firecrackers, during their peak, produced hundreds of thousands of yuan annually. Now, Hankou, Jingzhou, Shashi, Zhejiang, Guangdong, Foshan, and other ports have all been seized by Liuyang firecrackers. Zhangshu, Linjiang, Raozhou, and Leban have been seized by Xielu firecrackers. Ganzhou has been seized by Ji'an firecrackers. Currently, the only remaining sales market is a corner of Nanchang, with an annual output value of only over ten thousand yuan, and Zhejiang only has two or three tenths left. Therefore, we cable Your Association for review and request that you immediately forward this to the authorities for swift action to stop this, in order to relieve the suffering of the remaining people and maintain the real economy, which is of the utmost urgency. We await your response."

According to this, after the banditry in the county was suppressed, it was struck by a drought, the countryside is desolate, and the market is sluggish, which has reached its extreme. Now that the early rice harvest is near and the autumn harvest is expected, it is the time for recovery. However, the implementation of this matter will truly harm the places where work has been stopped. According to the information in the cable, we should cable for review and request that you forward this to the Ministry of Finance for swift correction, in order to ensure uniformity and compliance, and to avoid disappointment. We await your response."

Following this, we should cable Your Ministry for review and request swift orders to direct the Wanzai County Saltpeter and Sulfur Bureau to stop the heavy tax collection and continue to levy taxes according to previous regulations, in order to maintain the livelihoods of the common people, which is of the utmost importance.

Respectfully,

Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Commerce (with seal)

The Truth About the Ma Family Property Dispute

Ma Xiangbo has recently been involved in a lawsuit filed by his nephew's wife, Ma Lu, in court over property rights. The case has been heard again, with both parties' lawyers presenting their arguments in court. These events have been widely reported and have attracted attention from all sides, who believe that Ma, a highly respected man with virtue, who usually reveres religion and is enthusiastic about public welfare, and who even gave away his private farmland of four to five thousand mu to donate to an education fund, should not be involved in such a trivial matter to the point of litigation. In order to find out the truth, we conducted investigations from all sides. It is said that the old man had three brothers, with the old man being the second. They had already divided the family property and each received several thousand mu of inherited land. At that time, based on the division documents, each branch of the family allocated 300 mu of land as Ma's public property, which was only allowed to increase and not allowed to be mortgaged or sold. The annual income, in addition to covering the costs of repairing and viewing graves, commemorating and blessing ancestors, and helping orphans and widows, was entirely saved to add to the public property. Later, the old man donated all of his land and left nothing behind. The other two branches also gradually mortgaged and sold their land due to business failures over the years, leaving them with less than a thousand mu and in a precarious situation. The old man, as the clan leader, had a sense of responsibility to honor his ancestors and should be responsible for safeguarding the public property to prevent the gradual mortgaging and selling of it. Moreover, according to the will of Ding, the aunt of Lu, the eldest branch should also be supervised, and Lu had no right to interfere, let alone inherit or dispose of it, so there was no reason or possibility for the lawsuit. It is rumored that both sides hope to reach a settlement, but the old man's family absolutely denies this. The reason is that after Lu's husband, Xiaomei, died, he left behind heavy debts, and the widow and orphans are pitiful. Therefore, the income from this public property has been temporarily managed by the eldest branch, merely to supplement their needs, in order to fulfill the principle of helping oneself before helping others. Unexpectedly, Lu, instigated by others, falsely claimed it as private property in order to carry out her plan of occupying and selling it, resulting in the property rights dispute. It was not because Lu personally was unable to enjoy the income and property management that a settlement was needed or possible. Therefore, at the beginning of the dispute, although Zhang, Wang, and others were entrusted by the plaintiff to carry out mediation several times, no reasonable and concrete solution was reached, and the defendant side did not show any indication. Now that the litigation has begun, it is even more appropriate to wait quietly for the court's fair judgment. What was reported in the previous newspapers was by no means the truth. The facts are all there, and the truth will eventually be revealed.

A Major Fire Destroyed Houses at the Intersection of Maigen Road and Kader Road Yesterday Morning

The Entire Fulai Barber Shop Was Destroyed; Part of Yongfeng Fruit Shop Was Burned

The Fulai Barber Shop, opened by Li Dehong from Yangzhou at No. 32 Maigen Road (Intersection of Kader Road) in West Shanghai, suddenly caught fire at 4:30 yesterday morning due to carelessness. The fire was very fierce. After receiving the news from the patrolman, he urgently called the fire department. By the time the fire truck arrived, the fire was already out of control, and the floorboards had been pierced through. The sundries upstairs then fell down with a loud crash, shaking the neighborhood. Nearby residents were all awakened. Yongfeng Fruit Shop at No. 30 to the left was also affected by the fire at the time. For a time, the order was chaotic. The Xinzha Police Station sent Chinese and Western detectives to the scene to suppress the situation. It was not until after 6 o'clock that the fire was extinguished. The Fulai Barber Shop had been completely burned down, suffering the heaviest losses. Part of the Yongfeng Fruit Shop was burned. Fortunately, the shop staff all escaped, avoiding a tragedy. Afterwards, the fire starter, Li Dehong, was taken away by the Xinzha Police Station to investigate the cause of the fire. When the fire spread, the vegetable vendors who came early to the Kader Road vegetable market from the Shanban Factory and Xinqiao in Zhabei could not pass through, and the traffic north and south of the creek was blocked for quite some time.

Furthermore, Yang's apprentice, Hu Xiangsheng, claimed that he was in a dream when the fire broke out and was rescued, and he did not know anything else.
