Collision Incident of Two Public Buses: Responsibility Needs to Be Clarified Urgently; This Unfortunate Incident Happened After the Successful Closing of the National Games; Both Responsible Parties Released Statements Yesterday

—Rumors of Resignations by Zhang Dengyi and Jin Baoxian—

Everything at the National Games was going smoothly when a collision occurred between city-run and commercially-run public bus drivers on the closing day. The details have already been reported in yesterday's newspaper. The following is a continuation of the situation reported by a Central News Agency reporter:

Statement from the Responsible Party of the Municipal Public Works Bureau

According to the responsible party of the Municipal Public Works Bureau, after the opening of the National Games, the number of people coming and going increased sharply, and the existing Zhabei Chinese-run public buses were insufficient to meet the demand. Therefore, the bureau transferred a portion of the South Shanghai public buses to serve Zhabei. Unfortunately, on the closing day of the National Games, a collision occurred with the Chinese bus side. On the city-run bus side, in addition to Deputy Director Jin Baoxian being injured, five drivers and ticket sellers were also injured. Deputy Director Jin's injuries are relatively minor and he is temporarily resting. The other five people have all been sent to Qu Zhifu Hospital for treatment. Two of them are in critical condition. However, the occurrence of this incident was entirely due to a misunderstanding. In addition to reporting the details to the seventh-level authorities, the bureau also hopes that this matter will not be expanded.

Statement from the Responsible Party of the Chinese Bus Company

According to the responsible party of the Zhabei Chinese Public Bus Company, the company was very surprised by the unfortunate incident that occurred. Fortunately, the seven injured are not seriously injured. After being sent to Renji Hospital for treatment, their injuries have gradually lessened. However, the responsibility for the occurrence of this dispute still needs to be fairly investigated by the authorities. The company has now reported the details to the Municipal Public Works Bureau and informed the Long-Distance Bus Company Association to uphold justice. The company is particularly disturbed because the collision between the two sides frightened passengers and even caused injury. The company must solemnly express its regret. The truth of the matter will be judged fairly by society in the future. There is one more point that needs to be stated: it is rumored that the company dispatched a bus on the afternoon of that day carrying more than twenty drivers to the vicinity of East Sports Road to beat up the city-run bus drivers and ticket sellers. This is actually a misrepresentation. At that time, there was a shortage of vehicles for all departures, so how could there be extra vehicles?

Both Sides' Routes Return to Their Original State

Since yesterday, the South Shanghai Public Bus Management Office has ordered the buses temporarily transferred to Zhabei to return to their original routes in South Shanghai. The vehicles of the Zhabei Chinese Public Bus Company from Zhabei to the stadium have also been reduced and have returned to their original routes. Therefore, it can be hoped that this matter will not cause further disputes and cause anxiety to passengers.

The Municipal Public Works Bureau Discusses Response

Since the collision occurred the day before yesterday, Xu Peihuang, Director of the Municipal Public Works Bureau, immediately ordered the responsible personnel to investigate the details of the incident. The injured personnel of the city-run buses were sent to the hospital for treatment. Yesterday afternoon, he convened a temporary emergency meeting to discuss concrete measures to deal with this matter. However, the content of the measures has not yet been announced by the bureau. According to a reporter's inquiry from a certain source, the incident occurred during the National Games, so Zhang Dengyi, Section Chief of the Fourth Section of the Municipal Public Works Bureau and concurrently Director of the Transportation Division of the National Games, has reportedly offered his resignation. Jin Baoxian, Deputy Director of the Public Bus Management Office, was also present when the incident occurred. Unexpectedly, this unprecedented disaster was caused, and he has also expressed his intention to retire.

Zhang Dengyi's Written Statement

According to the written statement sent by the Public Works Bureau from Zhang Dengyi, Director of the Transportation Group of the National Games, the large number of spectators at this National Games was anticipated in advance. Therefore, the National Games consulted with the relevant bureaus of the city to prepare in advance. Except for the afternoon of October 10, when there were some difficulties due to rain, the other ten days were generally able to cope. This was all due to the assistance of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, the Public Safety Bureau, the Public Works Bureau, the Public Utilities Bureau, various public bus and long-distance bus companies, and various commercial car companies. I would like to express my sincere gratitude on behalf of the National Games. The collision between the drivers of the Chinese public buses and the city-run public buses on the closing day is very regrettable. Although Zhabei is the exclusive operating area of the Chinese Public Bus Company, the company does not have many vehicles. Usually, in the city center, when there are major events, transportation is already inconvenient. Therefore, for this grand event, it was expected that there would be many spectators and that the company's vehicles would not be able to cope. Therefore, the Shanghai-Minhang, Shanghai-Taicang, Shanghai-Songjiang, and Xihu Long-Distance Bus Companies and the City-run Public Bus Management Office were consulted in advance for assistance. A total of forty-seven vehicles were provided: six Shanghai-Taicang buses, three Shanghai-Minhang buses, one Shanghai-Songjiang bus, twenty Xihu buses, and seventeen city-run buses. This was to alleviate the transportation of the大会 and should not be regarded as competing for business. The four types of vehicles from Shanghai-Taicang, Shanghai-Minhang, Shanghai-Songjiang, and the city-run, drove on the same route, and the bus stops and routes at both ends have never been moved. The report that they were moved is not consistent with the facts. As for the report on the 21st that the overturning of a bus was due to the dissatisfaction of the citizens, it was reported that only the Chinese Public Bus Company had such an incident during the National Games. No other company's buses were reported to have caused incidents. Furthermore, the speed of vehicles traveling to and from the city center was limited by the large number of vehicles in front and behind, and they were mostly connected in a row. It was not possible for any particular vehicle to overtake other vehicles. As for the collision between the Chinese public bus and city-run public bus drivers, the Municipal Public Works Bureau is conducting a thorough investigation in order to deal with it fairly.

The Bride Commits Suicide After Returning to Her Maiden Home in Ningbo; A Pair of Scissors Was Stabbed Into Her Throat Because the Groom Was Disappointed Due to Her Blindness in One Eye

Cheng Baimei, a resident of Yu Family Lane, about half a li west of Yangjing Town, Pudong, had a son named Longsheng, who worked as a laborer. Since childhood, his parents had arranged a marriage through a matchmaker with Zhao Baba's daughter, Xinying, from the nearby area. Now that both the man and the woman have grown up and reached the age of marriage, they chose the 18th of this month according to the lunar calendar as the wedding date. At that time, they held a grand banquet and welcomed Zhao's daughter into their home. The next day (the day before yesterday) in the morning, according to local customs, the bride and groom should go to the bride's home to pay their respects, which is commonly called "returning to the maiden home." At about 4:00 PM, they still returned to the groom's home. Unexpectedly, after the bride entered the room, she closed the door tightly. The family thought she was changing clothes, so they did not suspect anything. At about 5:00 PM, when it was almost dinner time, there was still no movement in the room. They called out but received no response. The family was shocked and quickly tried to open the door. They saw the bride lying in a pool of blood. They found that a pair of scissors had been stabbed into her throat between her neck, deeply piercing about an inch and cutting off her throat. The scene was extremely tragic. They immediately reported to the Yangjing Police Station, which instructed the local security officer, Cheng Zhiwen, yesterday morning to report to the local court. In the afternoon, a prosecutor was dispatched to the scene to examine the body and determined that it was indeed a death caused by injury. They instructed the family to collect the body first and wait for interrogation. After this newlywed murder occurred, it caused a stir in the surrounding areas. As for the reason for the suicide, it was said that the bride had recently become blind in one eye due to illness, and the groom's family did not know about it. After she entered their home, the groom was very disappointed. The groom refused to go with her when she returned to her maiden home, and he did not pick her up afterwards, causing the bride to return alone. Therefore, she felt ashamed and took this drastic measure.

The Dental Association Holds an Oral Hygiene Exhibition, Which Started Yesterday

Various Tooth Models and Charts Are Displayed; The Exhibition Will Last for One Week and Visitors Are Welcome

In order to increase the public's knowledge of hygiene and raise awareness of dental health, the Shanghai Dental Association is holding the First Oral Hygiene Exhibition at the YMCA on North Sichuan Road for one week, starting yesterday. The hours are from 9:00 AM to 6:00 PM every day. The details are as follows:

Exhibition Begins: The Shanghai Dental Association, in view of the fact that the general public usually does not pay attention to oral hygiene, resulting in an increase in the number of people suffering from dental diseases, which has a significant impact on health, is holding the First Oral Hygiene Exhibition at the YMCA on Sichuan Road starting yesterday in order to increase the public's knowledge of hygiene and raise awareness of dental health. It started at 9:00 AM yesterday. The hours are from 9:00 AM to 6:00 PM every day. The exhibition will close after one week. All sectors are welcome to visit.

A Glimpse of the Display: The exhibition hall is located in the hall on the second floor of the YMCA on Sichuan Road. Slogans and pictures on oral hygiene and tooth care are hung all around. Various specially made models and real teeth are displayed in the hall, along with explanatory charts. The content can be divided into (1) the structure of teeth, (2) methods of protecting children's teeth during the growth period, (3) dental diseases, such as tooth decay, dental cystitis, and dental defects, and the treatment and prevention of other types of diseases caused by dental diseases, and (4) various methods of cleaning teeth and the oral cavity.

There Is No Malignant Malaria in Minhang

It was recently reported that malignant malaria was found in Minhang Town, Shanghai. The Shanghai County Government specially instructed the Minhang District Office to investigate and report in detail in order to take preventive measures. After receiving the order, District Chief Wu Shifang thoroughly investigated on one hand and sent a letter to the Chinese Medical Association for assistance on the other. According to the association's reply, the number of malaria cases in the statistical analysis of the cases of each member has increased compared with previous years. After treatment, most of them have recovered within a week, which seems to be a seasonal disease and there is no dangerous discovery. There are occasional cases where people who have malaria first develop other diseases, which seem to be more serious than ordinary malaria, but they are not life-threatening.

The Public Concession Bureau Begins Population Census

The population census in the Public Concession began today (Tuesday). Regarding the procedures and purpose of the census, the police stations had previously sent notification letters to each household. Starting today, the police stations will send blank population census forms to each household. If they cannot be delivered today, they will definitely be delivered early tomorrow morning, along with instructions on how to fill them out. Each household can fill them out in detail according to the instructions. The population census is common in various countries and in various parts of mainland China. It is used only for compiling population statistics and will not be used for other purposes. Residents within the concession are requested to fill out the blank forms promptly after receiving them and leave them for the census takers to collect.

10 Million Yuan Telecommunications Government Bonds: Mortgaged for 6 Million Yuan in Cash; Ministry Representatives Negotiating Smoothly in Shanghai; Banks in Shanghai Decide to Jointly Form a Syndicate to Underwrite the Loan

According to New News Agency, the Ministry of Communications, in order to develop international and domestic telecommunications and other transportation infrastructure, decided to issue 10 million yuan in telecommunications government bonds this year, mortgaging them to banks in Shanghai for 6 million yuan in cash at a 60% face value discount for distribution. Regarding this loan, the Minister of Communications, Zhu Jia Hua, entrusted the Director of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, Shen Shu Yu, to conduct preliminary negotiations with the banks. It is hoped that the agreement will become a reality. However, since the amount is quite large, it will be necessary for a number of banks to share the burden. Therefore, negotiations will take some time. In the future, in order to facilitate repayment, the underwriting banks will jointly form a syndicate to handle the matter. The representatives of the Ministry of Communications plan to convene a meeting of the underwriting banks to discuss the contract after the negotiations with each bank are completed. The current progress is quite smooth, and it is expected that the contract can be formally signed and payment can begin soon.

City Chamber of Commerce Answers Questions on Documents Subject to Stamp Tax

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce issued the following two letters yesterday to answer questions on documents subject to stamp tax:

Letter to Grain Depot: The Chamber replied to the Chambers of Commerce of Huian, Mei, and other towns, stating that it had received a letter dated the 19th of this month concerning the practice of grain merchants issuing depot receipts upon receiving rice for storage. These receipts are considered return receipts, and they are not used when the rice is retrieved in the future, so they are not collected and destroyed. The nature of these receipts differs from that of the depot slips used to retrieve goods. The Chamber inquired about which category of stamp tax should be applied. The Chamber checked Article 16, Clause 8 of the Stamp Tax Law, which lists "storage receipts" as a type of document. The nature column notes that all documents issued by stores, warehouses, or storage facilities to depositors for storing items are included. The nature of the depot receipts mentioned in the letter is the same as this clause, so it seems that stamp tax can be applied according to this clause. The Chamber is hereby informing you, and it is hoped that you will take note.

Temporary Goods Record Book: The Chamber replied to the West Gate National Goods Company in this city, stating that it had received a letter stating that the temporary goods record book, which is used for internal accounting and has no external relation, and contains no monetary figures, should not be subject to stamp tax. According to the Ministry of Finance's previous explanations, there is a distinction between internal and external documents, but account books are all used for internal auditing and are not used externally. Therefore, the old stamp tax regulations and the current stamp tax law both stipulate that if they are used for business, they should be subject to stamp tax, regardless of whether the account book records goods or money. The sample attached to the letter indicates the amount of goods received into the warehouse and the amount of goods paid to the retail department, which cannot be said to not be used for business. The inquiry that there is no need to pay stamp tax is a misunderstanding.

Trial Opens for Huangpu River Female Corpse Case: Prosecutor's Investigation Clear, Formal Indictment Filed; Qiao Qi Guilty of Joint Homicide

At 2:00 PM on August 3 of this year, when the Shengjing ship at Pier No. 3 of Swire Dock in the French Concession was leaving the port, the propeller stirred up a strange female corpse from the Huangpu River. The water police brought the corpse to the South Dock. A woman named Zhang Zhou Shi went to identify the body and confirmed that the deceased was her niece, Zhang Jin Lin. She then filed a lawsuit with the Procuratorate of the District Court, requesting a thorough investigation. Hao Zhong Yang, a dock worker, also reported to the water police that the deceased was pushed into the river and drowned, and he was willing to testify. The court ordered the police to accompany Hao Zhong Yang to the court and dispatched officers to take

Suspects

Qiao Qi Shi, Qiao Su Tang, Chu Fu Qing and others into custody. Qiao Qi Shi was detained after interrogation, and Qiao Lian Tang and others were released on bail pending further investigation. After further investigation, the situation became clear, and a criminal indictment was filed. The indictment stated that the defendant Qiao Qi Shi knew the deceased Zhang Jin Lin. Zhang Jin Lin originally had 2,000 silver dollars, which she had been depositing in Chu Fu Qing's comb shop. Two years ago, Zhang Jin Lin and her lover, whose surname was Meng,

Failed in Business

and returned to their native Shandong. This summer, Zhang Jin Lin returned to Shanghai alone to ask Chu Fu Qing to withdraw her deposits. Because she was in a hurry to leave, she did not bring her deposit book with her. Chu Fu Qing refused to pay. After several negotiations, Zhang Jin Lin published a notice in the newspaper stating that the deposit book was lost and withdrew 260 silver dollars. Later, the defendant persuaded Zhang Jin Lin to withdraw all of her deposits from Chu Fu Qing, claiming that the 260 silver dollars that had been withdrawn were interest on the deposits.

A Dispute Arose

with Chu Fu Qing. The defendant also asked a neighbor, Hu Yang Yuan, to introduce lawyer Hu Feng Lian to negotiate with Chu Fu Qing and mediate the dispute. The defendant often changed her tone when she organized Zhang Jin Lin to go out. At around 11:00 PM on August 2 of this year, the defendant, along with two unidentified men and one woman, used a yellow car to lure Zhang Jin Lin to the wharf on the Huangpu River with the premeditated intention of murdering her. Then, a man with a black mole on his leg took off Zhang Jin Lin's trousers and pushed her into the Huangpu River. Another man held a gun

To Prevent Outcries

The defendant and another woman sat by and watched. After Zhang Jin Lin was pushed into the river, the defendants fled. The next day, customs police recovered Zhang Jin Lin's body. An examination determined that she had indeed died from drowning. According to the testimony of the deceased's aunt, Zhang Zhou Shi, the defendant was arrested and questioned about the circumstances of the case and was prosecuted according to law. Although the defendant Qiao Qi Shi refused to admit to the joint homicide, Hao Zhong Yang's testimony was vivid and detailed. Moreover, the clothes that the defendant was wearing when she was arrested and the clothes and socks on Zhang Jin Lin's body were all preserved. However, her

Lower Body Was Without Trousers

This matched what Hao Zhong Yang had described. Combined with Zhang Zhou Shi's testimony that Zhang Jin Lin had previously said that the defendant would not let her out and that someone wanted to kill her, the defendant was indeed guilty of the crime under Article 271, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Judge Wu Xiang Zu opened the Thirteenth Court to hear the case. Attorney Fang Jun Jie, who had been appointed, appeared in court to defend the defendant. The judge ordered that Qiao Qi Shi, who was in custody, be brought to the court for questioning. She testified that she was 43 years old, from Yangzhou, and lived at No. 18 Huaixian Lane in the Old County Front.

Her Former Husband Was Deceased

She is currently having an affair with Qiao Lian Tang, the owner of Qiao Shun Chang Hat Shop. She met the deceased at a young ladies' home (i.e., Chu Fu Qing's home). She firmly denied the plot to murder Zhang Jin Lin. Then, Cheng Yong Nian, a detective from the water police station, recounted the events after the incident. Finally, Zhang Zhou Shi testified that she was 60 years old, from Shanghai, and lived at No. 2 Hengde Lane, Fuyou Road. Zhang Jin Lin was the daughter of her third sister and was her niece. She returned to Shanghai in early April and stayed at Qiao Qi Shi's house for a few days (Qiao Qi Shi is the sister-in-law of Chu Fu Qing's fourth concubine). On the night of the incident, around 9:00 PM, Zhang Jin Lin went outside to cool off at my house. I don't know how she was murdered. I request justice. After hearing the testimonies, the judge stated that the case was complex and would be continued at a later date. Qiao Qi Shi was returned to custody.

Mining and Finance Adjustment Committee: Review of Mining Merchants' Loans to be Completed Soon

To be Submitted to the Ministry for Approval for Lending by a Syndicate; Application Amount Exceeds the Allotment and Will Be Reduced Proportionally

In order to aid domestic mining, the Ministry of Industry established a 10 million yuan loan from the Shanghai Syndicate and established the Mining and Finance Adjustment Committee to oversee everything. The mining merchants have been applying for loans to the Ministry of Industry. The Ministry of Industry then handed over the application to the Mining and Finance Committee for examination. According to a New News Agency reporter, after the Mining Finance Committee has received the application forms and from the Industry Ministry, the Chief of the Technology Division Wang Zhengbu had dispatched experts to the mines for field investigation. The investigation is nearly complete. A committee meeting will be convened, after which the Ministry will be notified with the results for its approval. Then, each mining merchant will be notified to sign a contract directly with the syndicate according to the agreement that was set by the ministry. It has been heard that the total amount requested to be borrowed has exceeded ten million Yuan. It is now proposed that the syndicate should increase the amount borrowed. If the syndicate does not approve it, the Ministry will reduce the amount proportionally and it will be limited to ten million Yuan.

It specially purchased 1,000 bags of Fourth Grade flour from Fufeng Flour Company and sent them to Shanghai Flood Relief Association for fundraising in various provinces. The association has received letter saying, "We received a letter and were provided with a thousand sacks of flour with a shipping order from Fufeng Flour Factory. It shows your concern for the victims and your zeal for disaster relief, we are extremely grateful. We have drawn a receipt and given it to the messenger, please check it, it will be sent to Shandong. Lu Chabohu, the director of this association, will select the worst-hit areas to receive the donation."

Hubei Provincial Party Department Launches an Exhibition of Calligraphy, Paintings, and Antiques to Raise Funds for Relief

Ai Minying, Liu Minggao, Yu Yuzhi, Tao Yaojie and others from the Hubei Provincial Committee, were concerned about the disaster in central Hubei and launched the Hubei Calligraphy, Painting and Antiques Exhibition to Aid Disaster Relief. The solicitation for works stated that: "Hubei Province is unfortunate. It has suffered disasters three times in four years, and the vast area affected by the disaster this year and the large number of disaster victims are even greater than the floods of 1920 and the drought of 1923. Families have been ruined and washed away by floods. The remaining people have been displaced, lacking clothing and food. Therefore, all that can be heard is the cry of hunger and cold, and all that can be seen is the tragic situation of the old and the young being carried away. We have seen this and specially launched the Hubei Calligraphy, Painting and Antiques Exhibition to Aid Disaster Relief. We will collect works by famous calligraphers and painters from ancient and modern times and valuable antiques from private collections for exhibition and sale. We hope to use the funds raised from the exhibition and sale to provide disaster relief. We hope that people from all walks of life will support this righteous cause, either by donating their own works to society or by generously donating their treasured collections, or even by temporarily lending them for exhibition. If you agree, please send your works to the office of the association in the Hubei Provincial Party Department by the end of November. We look forward to receiving your works." The Preparatory Committee includes He Chengjun, Zhang Qun, Xia Douyin, Fang Benin, Yu Yuzhi, and others. It is heard that the association has also hired Wang Shijie, Ju Zheng, Wu Xingya, and more than 20 others as preparatory committee members and is widely soliciting works from all circles in Beijing and Shanghai.

China Communications and Six Other Banks Invest in Zhejiang Provincial Fishery Cooperative

According to China East News Agency, in order to support the production and sales of the fishing industry in Dinghai Shenjiamen, the Zhejiang Construction Department has specially contacted and guided the local fishermen to organize a fishery cooperative. The capital is 600,000 yuan, with the entire production of the local fishing depots as collateral. The local financial circles will underwrite 300,000 yuan, and the remaining half has been approved by the Construction Department from various banks. The Bank of China in this city had previously invested in the fishing industry at the behest of the Director, Chen Gongbo, and therefore actively approved the investment. The six banks, namely the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Zhejiang Local Bank, the China Industrial Bank, the Shanghai Siming Bank, and the China Farmers' Bank, each invested 50,000 yuan. The contract can be formally signed within the next few days.

Dongtai Business Tax Bureau: Forced Cotton Tax Causes Repercussions; Cotton Mill Association Cables Finance Department to Intervene

The Chinese Cotton Mill Association telegraphed the Jiangsu Finance Department yesterday, stating: "To the esteemed Zhao, Director of the Zhenjiang Finance Department: According to letters from Changzhou Dacheng Textile Company and Wuxi Mofeng Textile Company, our mills have established cotton purchasing offices in Datongji, Dongtai, to purchase raw materials solely for our own use. This was previously approved by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, which issued branch licenses, and was also submitted to the Jiangsu Finance Department for record-keeping. Now, according to letters from our cotton purchasing offices, the local Business Tax Bureau has repeatedly demanded the payment of business tax since the new cotton crop was introduced this year and purchasing began. Despite presenting the Ministry of Industry and Commerce licenses and Finance Department approvals, they were ignored and transport permits were denied, preventing the transport of already purchased cotton. Their intention is to make it difficult for the mills to meet their needs, forcing them to comply with their coercive demands. They have even threatened to collect taxes directly from farmers in front of the cotton purchasing offices if they cannot obtain them from the offices. Our mill's cotton purchasing offices in Datongji fully comply with the Ministry's regulations on exempting cotton purchasing offices of cotton mills from business tax and the Department's regulations on auditing and exempting cotton mill cotton purchasing offices from business tax. There is absolutely no obligation to pay business tax. Moreover, farmers who grow and sell their own cotton have no reason to pay business tax. This contradicts the intention of protecting farmers, and our mills will suffer unexpected losses. Therefore, we respectfully submit this letter, requesting you to forward it for intervention and issue transport permits according to regulations, to maintain the law and alleviate commercial difficulties, etc." The message continues, "We have investigated that the two factories have set up purchasing stations in the production area to purchase cotton, and have complied with the Ministry's orders and the Department's regulations on exempting business tax. However, the Business Tax Bureau still enforces the law with undue strictness, even collecting taxes directly from cotton farmers in front of the cotton purchasing offices. This is no different from treating business tax as likin, which is prohibited by law. We earnestly request you to promptly issue strict warnings to the business tax bureaus of various counties and to refrain from further harassing the cotton purchasing offices of various textile companies, in order to maintain the rule of law and alleviate commercial difficulties. We await your urgent command."

Collapsing House During Demolition; Scrap Collector Severely Injured

At 5:30 PM yesterday at number 408 Hankou Road, the tenant of the kitchen in that house intended to dismantle the partition for sale. They summoned Lu Jigen (28 years old) and Dai Lisheng (56 years old), two men from Jiangbei who regularly collect scrap, residing at number 8, Dajing Road, Xiaobeimen, Nanshi. After agreeing on a price, Lu and Dai began to dismantle the partition. Unexpectedly, due to years of disrepair, the upper pavilion lost its center as soon as the partition was removed. With a crash, it collapsed from above, burying Dai and Lu in the decaying wood and broken tiles. Lu Jigen suffered head and shoulder injuries that were not serious, but Dai Lisheng suffered severe injuries throughout his body. Someone reported the incident to the police station, who dispatched officers to transport the two men to Renji Hospital for treatment.

Spring and Autumn

(Snippets)

— (Rustic Elder)

Remembering the drastic changes in the world and the great disaster of today, even with outstanding talents, it is difficult to reverse the turbulent tide. Those who believe in fate consider it the Jiazi year of the lower cycle; those who worry unnecessarily only lament in vain. I believe that "The Book of Changes" says, "When things reach an end, they change; when they change, they flow; when they flow, they endure." This is an unchanging teaching, so why be sad!

The Song Dynasty was destroyed by the Yuan Dynasty, and the Ming Dynasty was destroyed by the Qing Dynasty. For hundreds of years, the vast Chinese territory was lost to foreign peoples. However, they all soon restored the old order and returned our rivers and mountains. Now, some people console themselves with this, which is a great mistake. Are not Korea and Taiwan lost forever? Today's situation is different, and the methods of subjugation are harsher. How should the people of the country save themselves?

Our country is like a rich, elderly widow. Person A, a charlatan, covets her wealth and seduces her. Fearing that charlatans B and C will interfere, he treats them as forbidden topics, jealous and threatening in every way. Alas, the situation of this rich, elderly widow is truly precarious!

Looking broadly at historical mirrors, both Chinese and foreign, we can see the causes of rise and fall, success and failure. How should the court and the people encourage themselves?

Ancestral Shrine of Cotton

— Rong Yu

Looking at the cotton cloth I am wearing, I am reminded of Huang Daopo, who first planted cotton in Shanghai.

Huang Daopo lived at the end of the Yuan Dynasty. Her hometown was Wunijing in Shanghai. She lived in the Fujian and Guangdong areas for some time and secretly learned the methods of planting cotton and weaving cloth from the locals. When she returned to Shanghai, she brought back many cotton seeds. In addition to planting them herself, she also distributed the seeds to others and taught them the methods of spinning and weaving. In this way, women in the surrounding villages learned how to spin and weave. This indeed found a productive industry for women, and her contribution was truly great. Later generations did not forget her merits and built an ancestral shrine of cotton to commemorate her.

However, I saw in a textbook published by a certain bookstore that the Ancestral Shrine of Cotton is now abandoned and cannot be traced. This is somewhat incorrect. According to records, the Ancestral Shrine of Cotton is located behind the Longmen Academy in the west gate of Shanghai. The main hall has a veranda, and four phoenix trees are planted in the courtyard. In the center of the hall is a statue of Huang Daopo with a kind and gentle face, demonstrating her achievement of benefiting the people. Two maids are sculpted on either side, standing respectfully. Later, the Longmen Academy was converted into a normal school. Due to insufficient school buildings, the site of the shrine was included in the school. However, the main hall and the statue of the god were not damaged in the slightest. Several flat houses were built in front of the hall to serve as sickrooms for the students. The main hall served as a dining hall for the patients. The remaining houses on both sides were used as residences for the school staff. In this way, the shrine was isolated from the outside world, and it was not well known or accessible. After 1927, the normal school buildings were converted into the junior high school of the Shanghai Provincial Middle School, and the shrine was still included in the school's sphere of influence. Last year, after the Shanghai Middle School moved into its new campus, the entire original campus was auctioned off, and the Ancestral Shrine of Cotton was of course included. However, a group of protectors of ancient sites proposed that the Ancestral Shrine of Cotton be demarcated, repaired, and maintained. It is not known whether this will be implemented.

Opening Remarks

— Feng Moni

Everyone who works in society needs to understand opening remarks. What are opening remarks? They are the meaningless, trivial greetings you exchange with friends when you meet, the so-called perfunctory remarks, which are also opening remarks.

It is certainly not good for two people to meet and remain silent like mutes. Therefore, there must be opening remarks to perfunctorily fill the silence. However, some people's opening remarks are somewhat comical. For example, someone goes to the latrine to relieve himself and meets an acquaintance, and says, "You're relieving yourself!" The other person replies, "You're relieving yourself too!" Because they both need to relieve themselves, they both come to the latrine. There is definitely no one who has the leisure to go to the latrine to smell the fragrance of wood buds, and no one with such a good appetite. Such perfunctory opening remarks seem too humorous.

Some people go to the bathhouse to take a bath and see a friend lying naked on the couch. They still perfunctorily say, "Are you bathing?" (Wu dialect) Thinking carefully, it is truly laughable to foreigners. No one in the world is so foolish as to admire antiques in a bathhouse as if it were a museum. Such perfunctory opening remarks are really unacceptable.

The term "opening remarks" comes from the fact that when actors come on stage in the theater, they do not start singing immediately, but first play an introductory tune, and then sit down and recite four lines of poetry. This is called the "opening remarks." Today, people think that saying the first words to someone is called "opening remarks."

I am not good at meaningless perfunctory remarks and do not understand the mystery of opening remarks. When I see a friend, I actually get dizzy, which means I understand the meaningless perfunctory opening remarks, but I still can't bring myself to say them, because they are really meaningless empty words.

Though a door is set, it is often closed

Same Rooftop

— (Drunken Woodcutter)

People in the city seem to be tired of living on the ground, so they have started rooftop gardens, rooftop dance halls, rooftop movie theaters, and rooftop wine shops. In general, young men and women are all carefree and happy on the rooftops. But when we look at the tragic situation in the disaster areas, countless suffering people are waiting for rescue on the rooftops, sleeping on the rooftops, and weeping on the rooftops. The white waves on the ground rise to the sky, but they cannot get down to the ground. In contrast, the same rooftops are one of gilded pleasure and the other of heartbreaking misery! I hope that the people in the city, while enjoying themselves on the rooftops, will think of the refugees on the rooftops in the disaster areas and generously donate to help them. That would be truly meritorious!... This is what Yangzhou storyteller Wang Shaotang told us on the East China Radio Station. At the same time, I also hope that all radio stations can promote this in the same way!

Little Western Paradise

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 20: Scrambling for Life to See Grandson; Embracing Each Other and Weeping; Remembering the Past in the Famine Year; Sowing Wheat and Inviting Disaster

He smiled at them and said, "If there is anything, let your daughter tell me slowly. "As he spoke, he turned to Yueying and said, "Just tell me. Maybe I can help you a little." Yueying looked at her grandmother and said, "Grandma, you can lie on that bed for a while. We paid money to rent this room, and everything in this room today is ours." Zhu Hushi walked forward and supported her, saying, "Mother! You are not feeling well, so you should lie down!" Old Lady Zhu followed her daughter-in-law's support, and her body fell downward, her hand supporting the soft, sunken rattan backing of the bed. She grabbed Zhu Hushi's clothes in fright and sat up again. Yueying said, "It's okay for now. It's more comfortable for you to lie down than in our earthen kiln!" Mrs. Zhou said, "Don't worry about them. Tell me your story." Seeing that her grandmother was already lying down and her mother was sitting on the edge of the bed, Yueying first sighed and said to Mrs. Zhou, "We are not low-class people who sell our children." We used to farm and raise livestock in Gansu and lived a very peaceful life. My father left us when he was only thirty-eight years old." Hearing about her husband, Zhu Hushi immediately shed two lines of tears like two thick crystal threads, falling straight down. She choked and said, "He didn't leave us! He was taken away by soldiers and tortured to death." Yueying straightened her face and said, "Mother, why are you so ignorant? This Mrs. Zhou..." As she spoke, her eyes looked at Mrs. Zhou with a look of terror. Mrs. Zhou smiled and said, "It doesn't matter. I am not a soldier. Just tell me your story. Even if I were a soldier, the soldier you are talking about is not necessarily me. Why would I blame you? Just tell me whatever you want to say." (345)

御香縹緲錄

— Original work by Princess Der Ling of Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Chapter 35: Ominous Signs

This deep autumn of the year was truly a special season that one could never forget. After September, the days gradually shortened, and the leaves on various trees began to fall. We, a group of people who had lived in the sacred palace for a long time, originally did not pay much attention to the change of each season, but this time we all felt a strange sensation. Although no one could clearly say what the reason was, everyone indeed felt it, especially the Empress Dowager herself. Perhaps it could be said that as the weather gradually cooled in late autumn, people's skin would naturally have a different feeling, which would also cause a corresponding reaction in their hearts. This explanation seemed reasonable, but we had certainly encountered the atmosphere of late autumn before, and why hadn't it had any impact in previous years, but this year suddenly caused this feeling? Moreover, the stimulation of this feeling was extremely sharp, making us feel uneasy all day long, as if great difficulties and great terror were about to befall us soon. However, everyone was only worried in secret and dared not express anything in words.

It wasn't until this incident happened that we realized that our palpitations were the most accurate premonition!

How exactly did this incident start? I only recalled it after the fact.

Among the flowers and trees in the imperial garden, the magnolia (i.e., jade magnolia) was not considered a rare or exotic variety, but there were still dozens of them planted. Every early summer, they would bloom with many flowers. It was just because they didn't have any special characteristics that we never paid much attention to them. By late spring, we would not easily glance at them. (441)

Rambling Remarks

Further Discussion on Shop Signs

— Yan Fusun

There is a grocery store in Shanghai's West District named "勃郎林" (Bólánglín), which can be considered peculiar. As far as I know, there is also a Chaozhou confectionery store named "勃郎林" (Bólánglín) at the intersection of Guangdong Road and Shilu Road, facing each other from afar, which is a rare coincidence. On Baoxing Road in Zhabei, there is also a biscuit shop with a sign that says "轟天雷" (Hōngtiānléi, Thunderous Bomb). There was also a laundry shop in Caojiadu that has already closed, named "一口劍" (Yīkǒu jiàn, One-Mouth Sword), which was bizarre and incredible, simply baffling.

A few years ago, there was even a joke in Zhabei, where there was a tin foil shop that almost had a vulgar name. Suddenly, a new shop sign was erected at the entrance of the shop, with the eleven large characters "上海冥國銀行鈔票發兌處" (Shànghǎi Míngguó Yínháng Chāopiào Fādùichù, Shanghai Underworld National Bank Note Exchange Office) written on it. Shanghai is directly under the Underworld, and the Underworld is parasitic in Shanghai. A financial institution that connects humans and ghosts like this may have a day of realization in five hundred years. After all, the times are different, and everyone thought it appeared too early. The government was furious, and the Underworld Bank was declared liquidated. As for the so-called banknotes, they have not been cashed to this day, and I'm afraid they have all been turned into ashes together with the tin foil.

Shanghai is full of travel agencies, with various names, too numerous to list. Among them, the more meaningful ones, in my opinion, are the following two. One is "源源" (Yuányuán, Source Source) on Second Ma Road, which takes the meaning of inexhaustible. It is both popular and elegant. One is "香賓" (Xiāngbīn, Champagne) on Third Ma Road (recently closed), Running Horse Champagne, everyone already has a deep impression in their minds. Now, the two characters "香檳" (Xiāngbīn, Champagne) are used homophonously as "香賓" (Xiāngbīn, Fragrant Guest), which is already clever, and the fledgling guests are all popular figures. There is a line in the rustic ancient style: "Guests arrive like fragrant liqueur", the two characters "香賓" (Xiāngbīn, Fragrant Guest) are even more poetic, and that feels extra flavorful.

Shanghai's pawnshops and pawnshops account for the most broken records in the national statistics. Walking out of the streets and alleys, you can meet Mr. "尚" (Shàng, Still) and Mr. "田" (Tián, Field) everywhere. The names of the pawnshops, with the two signs "兩濟" (Liǎngjì, Two Reliefs) and "兩宜" (Liǎngyí, Two Suitable), are the most accurate. The principle of benefiting others and benefiting oneself can be taken into account. There is a small pawnshop in Zhabei with a golden sign of "民生" (Mínshēng, People's Livelihood), which obviously takes the meaning of relieving the people's livelihood and implying adjusting finance. The intention is of course not blameworthy, but the elements of people's livelihood completely depend on Mr. Shang and Mr. Tian as the source of life. Temporarily fortunately "生" (Shēng, Live), but eventually tend to "死" (Sǐ, Die). Sure enough, during the January 28th Incident, the enemy's iron island's poisonous bomb shattered the entire people's livelihood sign.

Shanghai also has a strange kind of medium sign, less than five inches wide and less than one foot long. It looks small and insignificant, but its seductiveness is unmatched by any other shop sign. These small shop signs, according to the formula of birds of a feather flock together, are like scales and combs, either in the neighborhood of "羣玉清和" (Qúnyù qīnghé, A gathering of jade, pure and harmonious) or in the lane of "福致勤之" (Fú zhì qín zhī, Happiness comes from diligence). The strangeness of the so-called strange shop signs is often the crystallization of the talents of the foreign field. I once took a quick look and noticed three colorful banners. One is "奇俠" (Qíxiá, Strange Knight), one is "虫二閣" (Chóng èr gé, Insect Two Pavilion), and one is "非非" (Fēifēi, Non-Non). These names seem to be as mysterious as "勃郎林" (Bólánglín) and "一口劍" (Yīkǒu jiàn) on the shop signs. After I racked my brains, I finally captured them all in one fell swoop, without missing a single one. It turns out that the two characters "奇俠" (Qíxiá, Strange Knight) are dissected using my gourd fortune-telling method. It just turns into the four characters "大可夾人" (Dà kě jiā rén, Greatly able to trap people), an absolutely wonderful phrase, which can be called vicious. The two characters "虫" (Chóng, Insect) and "二" (Èr, Two) are suspected of being a symbol of boundless romance, which is also interesting. What makes people spit out tea is the screen of the literary tiger of the two characters "非非" (Fēifēi, Non-Non). The riddle of "非非" (Fēifēi, Non-Non) is "想入" (Xiǎng rù, Think enter). When connected to form a sentence, it is "想入非非" (Xiǎng rù fēifēi, Indulge in fantasies). People who indulge in fantasies can really be regarded as indulging in fantasies. I think Miss "非非" (Fēifēi, Non-Non) will definitely be unable to laugh or cry after reading this wonderful article.

Finally! I would also like to add a statement that I rely on selling articles and fortune-telling for a living, and the Ronglu fortune-telling that I created has been around for exactly ten years. The gourd question is located in the New World Hotel, only this one, and there are no branches. Recently, a friend from Hong Kong wrote to inform me that there is also "嚴鞭孫葫蘆測字" (Yán biān sūn húlu cèzì, Yan Bian Sun's Gourd Fortune-telling) in Hong Kong, and also stated that they came to Hong Kong from Shanghai. In fact, I have never left Shanghai. The Yan Bian Sun in Hong Kong is of course someone else. Sima Xiangru, whose name is Xiangru, is actually not Xiangru. I dare not steal the beauty of others. Because I have received inquiries from relatives and friends in Hong Kong and Guangdong, I will answer it incidentally. Also, there is also "嚴芙蓀測字" (Yán fú sūn cèzì, Yan Fu Sun's Fortune-telling) in Caojiadu in this city. (A grass head is added above the character "孫" (Sūn, Sun), which is a difference). There is also "小葫蘆測字" (Xiǎo húlu cèzì, Small Gourd Fortune-telling) in Nanyang Bridge, which has nothing to do with me, alas! Poor me! The difficulty of begging for food as a writer, I really can't bear to write any more.

Sports News

Corrections to National Games Announced Yesterday: Men's Swimming and Women's Tennis Rankings Adjusted; Men's Tennis Unchanged Due to "Valid Reasons"; Prizes Already Claimed, Re-Packed for Distribution

The rankings and scores for men's and women's tennis and men's swimming announced at the 6th National Games contained errors. This newspaper made corrections yesterday. After these errors in swimming scores and women's tennis rankings were discovered, it was decided to correct them yesterday. However, regarding the men's tennis rankings, it was stated that there were no errors because the Games had its own views and reasons.

Corrected Men's Swimming Rankings

The organizing committee officially announced the corrected men's swimming scores yesterday. The Central News Agency issued the following announcement: "There were slight errors in the calculation of the scores for men's and women's swimming at this National Games. The Records Department of the Games hereby corrects them as follows:"

Men's Swimming Women's Swimming

Guangdong 57 points, won the championship Guangdong 62 points, won the championship

Hong Kong 50 points, won the second place Hong Kong 40 points, won the second place

Malaya 31 points, won the third place Guangxi 15 points, won the third place

Shanghai 12 points, won the fourth place Nanjing 3 points, won the fourth place

According to the above corrections, Shanghai is fourth in the men's swimming overall score, previously incorrectly reported as Guangxi. Therefore, Shanghai should get 27 points for the men's overall championship, while Guangxi has no points.

Corrected Women's Tennis Rankings

The errors in the women's tennis rankings were also first discovered by this newspaper. The fourth place should be Sichuan, not Malaya. After investigating the records, Sichuan got third in the women's doubles, and Malaya got fourth. Therefore, the first place is Shanxi, the second place is Shanghai, the third place is Nanjing, and the fourth place should be Sichuan. A prize has been notified to the prize department to be sent to Sichuan. Malaya had already claimed it. Men's swimming will also send a copy to Shanghai, as the silversmith had given it to Guangxi.

Reasons for Men's Tennis Rankings

As for the reasons for the men's tennis rankings, the Games' reasons are stated as follows: Whether it is fair or not, let's not discuss it for the moment. It is said that the determination of the tennis championship depends on the performance of a unit in singles and doubles. The singles and doubles must be good. Sichuan got fourth place in both singles and doubles, while Malaya only got third place in doubles and no ranking in singles. Therefore, Sichuan should be above Malaya. According to this statement, if one unit gets first place in singles and another unit gets two second places, the championship should belong to the latter. This point of Malaya's is related to the overall championship ranking, which involves too much, and it may not be convenient to correct it.

Errors Corrected in the General Report

The errors in the Games' score reports will be corrected in the general report. The Records Department issued a message yesterday stating that due to the urgency of time, there may be errors in the records of various events of the Games, which are not easy to correct. Therefore, the official results of the Games should be based on the Games' general report.

National Games Jury Committee Discusses Shanghai and Beijing Protests Yesterday; Beijing Protests Shanghai Athlete Wei Dingyi; Resolution: Both Cases Require Further Investigation

During the National Games, Shanghai protested that Nanjing athlete Yang Chunfu participated in the preliminary elections of two units. The jury committee held a meeting and decided to conduct an investigation. It is now known that the photos have been sent from Zhenjiang. The jury committee convened a meeting in the National Games Secretariat yesterday, with Wang Zhengting acting as chairman. At the same time, Beijing also protested that Shanghai men's volleyball player Wei Dingyi also participated in the Jiangsu preliminary election, requesting disqualification. The jury committee discussed the results and considered that the case still needs to be investigated. If the Games Organizing Committee ends, the findings will be reported to the Ministry of Education for approval.

Overseas Chinese Athletes Participating in the National Games to Go to Beijing for Sightseeing by Early Train Tomorrow Morning; Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission Sends Special Commissioner to Accompany and Receive the Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau

Among the overseas Chinese who returned to the country to participate in the National Games this time, there are three units: Malaya, the Philippines, and Java. The Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, in order to treat overseas Chinese preferentially, has sent a special commissioner to Shanghai to meet with Mr. Jian Jinglun, director of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau of this city, to receive all the athletes from the three units of Malaya, the Philippines, and Java to go to Beijing for sightseeing. It has been decided that they will leave Shanghai for Beijing by early express train tomorrow morning (22nd), stay for about a week, and then return to Shanghai.

Yesterday's Charity Swimming Performance: Liu Baoxi Breaks National Backstroke Record with a Time of 1 Minute, 19.1 Seconds

The charity swimming performance competition for the disaster-stricken people in various regions, organized by the All-China Games swimming athletes, was held at the city pool yesterday at 2:15 PM. In addition to the ten scheduled events, impromptu additions included high board diving and various butterfly stroke performances, all of which were highly entertaining. Liu Baoxi, the hero from the South, and Yang Xiuqiong, the "Mermaid," lived up to expectations by setting new records. However, the audience was only about 1,000 people, far fewer than the enthusiasm of the previous few days. Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan, and Xu Shiying, chairman of the various provincial flood relief committees, all graced the pool to watch the competition. The atmosphere at the poolside was quite heated, and the audience erupted in cheers at every exciting moment. The "Guoguang" reporter's detailed report on yesterday's competition is as follows:

Li Luomin Benefits from Sprint

The opening act yesterday was the men's 100-meter freestyle, a gathering of elites. It began at 2:27 PM with an air temperature of 77 degrees and a water temperature of 69 degrees. The participants included Shen Dingpeng from Malaya, Li Luomin from Hong Kong, Shi Jinpei from Guangdong, and Ren Mengxiong, also from Guangdong. Chen Zhenxing was unable to participate due to not finishing changing clothes. The starter, Guan Songsheng, held his gun ready to fire. Ren and Shi started early, and Commander Guan enforced the rules strictly, calling them back for a restart. The first two swimmers had already swam half a lap. After the restart, the strength of all four swimmers was equal in the first leg, with no clear leader. Shen Dingpeng's nimble turn gave him the lead, but Li Luomin's sprint was even better. At 75 feet, he surpassed Dingpeng and raced straight to the finish line, taking the lead by four feet. Shi from Guangdong followed closely in third place, four feet behind, with Ren from Guangdong in last place. The time was 1 minute, 11.8 seconds. At that time, the mayor was seated high on the podium, frequently asking if a record had been broken. However, due to the two starts with no rest in between, the competitors were physically exhausted; otherwise, a record might have been broken.

1. Li Luomin (Hong Kong) 1 minute, 11.8 seconds

2. Shen Dingpeng (Malaya) 1 minute, 13.6 seconds

3. Shi Jinpei (Guangdong)

4. Ren Mengxiong (Guangdong)

"Mermaid" Shows Skills in Women's 50 Feet

The second event was the women's 50-meter freestyle, with participants Sa Huiying, Chen Yuhui, and Yang Xiuqiong. To increase the interest, Huiying started one second before Yuhui, and Xiuqiong started five seconds later, to see if the "Mermaid" could catch up. After the gun fired, Huiying jumped into the water. Commander Guan silently counted the seconds beside her. At one second, he pushed Yuhui into the water. After another four seconds, he patted the "Mermaid's" tail and she leaped out with a splash. By that time, Huiying had already swam 20 meters, and Yuhui was not far behind Sa. The "Mermaid" was indeed miraculously skilled. As the water splashed, she surpassed Yuhui within 30 meters, earning a near-frantic cheer from the audience on both sides of the pool. The "Mermaid" increased her speed again, racing to the finish line. Huiying was also capable, and despite the strong opponent behind her, she calmly sprinted to the finish. Sa's hand touched the edge of the pool first, not allowing her to catch up, but the difference between them was only the height of a hand, not even an inch. Xiuqiong's time was 37 seconds flat, breaking her own national record of 38 seconds, but not matching her best time of 36 seconds in the All-China Games this year. The results are as follows:

1. Sa Huiying (Hong Kong) 43.2 seconds

2. Yang Xiuqiong (Hong Kong) 37 seconds (Breaks National Record)

3. Chen Yuhui (Hong Kong) 43.7 seconds

Baoxi's Backstroke Skills are Astonishing

The men's 100-meter backstroke is Hong Kong's Liu Baoxi's specialty. He is considered the best in the country, with no one to challenge him. He arrived too late to participate in the All-China Games this time, and yesterday's charity competition was his first chance to show his skills. As expected, he made a splash, breaking the national record and the All-China Games record. It was truly commendable. Only four participants took part in this event yesterday: Lin Fuyu from Malaya, Shi Jinpei from Guangdong, Chen Qiqian from Hong Kong, and Liu. After the start, Liu's arms moved like lightning. At 20 meters, Liu had already taken the lead by five feet. Although Lin Fuyu tried hard to catch up, Liu was fifteen or sixteen feet ahead when they turned at 50 meters. Baoxi's speed was not only astonishing, but his swimming style was also the most modern rotating style. His body was exceptionally agile when he turned. His final speed was so fast that it was almost perfect. He finished seventeen meters ahead of Fuyu, with Shi more than ten feet behind Lin. The time was 1 minute, 19.1 seconds, breaking his own national record of 1 minute, 23.1 seconds and the All-China Games record of 1 minute, 23.5 seconds held by Lin Huijun from Malaya. The results are as follows:

(Breaks National and All-China Games Records)

1. Liu Baoxi (Hong Kong) 1 minute, 19.1 seconds

2. Lin Fuyu (Malaya) 1 minute, 36 seconds

3. Shi Jinpei (Guangdong)

4. Chen Qiqian (Hong Kong)

Xiuqiong Enters the Water Swiftly as an Arrow

Only the Yang sisters participated in the women's 100-meter freestyle. To maintain her strength, the "Mermaid" expressed her willingness to start nine seconds after Xiuzhen. When Xiuqiong entered the water, Xiuzhen had already swam past the 22-meter line. Many spectators on both sides of the pool were worried for the "Mermaid." Director Pan also said that the disadvantage was too great, and she might not be able to catch up. However, the "Mermaid" possessed exceptional skills. She leaped forward, swiftly as an arrow. When she turned at 50 meters, she was only five or six meters behind Zhen. The "Mermaid" swam faster and faster. At 90 meters, she had already passed Xiuzhen and taken the lead. She finished first, beating Zhen by three feet. The applause was thunderous, and the cheers sounded like a stampede of ten thousand horses. The time was 1 minute, 23.5 seconds, breaking her own national and Far East Games record. It was only 0.5 seconds slower than Yang's time at the All-China Games this year. It was extremely commendable and could only be achieved with true skill.

1. Yang Xiuqiong 1 minute, 23.5 seconds (Breaks National and Far East Records)

2. Yang Xiuzhen 1 minute, 37.1 seconds

Luomin Triumphs in the 400 Meters

The participants in the men's 400-meter freestyle were Wu Wenjian from Malaya, Shi Jinpei from Guangdong, and Li Luomin from Hong Kong. Their strengths seemed evenly matched at first. In the first two laps, they were neck and neck, swimming in a straight line. When turning at the third lap, Shi used his feet to push off the wall, slightly taking the lead. Li and Wu then strove forward, and at 250 feet, the two were neck and neck, leading by more than ten feet. In the final lap, Li Luomin relied on his agile turns to shake off Wenjian and accelerated his sprint, reaching the finish line in a blink of an eye, defeating Wu by about nine feet. Jinpei's strength waned, and he finished more than a foot behind Wu. The results are as follows:

1. Li Luomin (Hong Kong) 6 minutes, 28.7 seconds

2. Wu Wenjian (Malaya) 6 minutes, 37.1 seconds

3. Shi Jinpei (Guangdong)

Hong Kong Wins the Four-Stroke Relay

The men's 200-meter relay was temporarily changed to a four-stroke relay, in the form of a Hong Kong-Guangdong contest. In the first leg, Hong Kong was represented by Liu Baoxi, and Guangdong by Su Tianmo. In the second leg, the breaststroke, Hong Kong was represented by Chen Fuxing, competing against Guangdong's "Frog King" Guo. In the third leg, the sidestroke, Hong Kong's Zeng Hefu met Guangdong's Chen Qisong. In the fourth leg, the freestyle, Hong Kong used Li Luomin, and Guangdong used Ren Mengxiong. At the sound of the gun, Liu and Su leaned back and swam forward. How could Baoxi's throne be usurped? He beat Su by more than five feet. In the second leg, Hong Kong's Chen Fuxing started first, with "Frog King" Guo trailing by five or six feet. Midway, the "Frog King" displayed his exceptional skills, gradually closing in. In the end, the disadvantage was too great, and Fuxing was not a weakling either. At the end of the second leg, the Guangdong team was still more than two feet behind. In the third leg, the sidestroke, Hefu was stronger than Qisong, leading by another four feet. In the final leg, the freestyle, Mengxiong and Luomin fought fiercely. Luomin took the lead first, and with the advantage he had from the first three legs, he easily won. The results are as follows:

Leg 1 Leg 2 Leg 3

(Hong Kong Team) Liu Baoxi (Backstroke) Chen Fuxing (Breaststroke) Zeng Hefu (Sidestroke)

Leg 4

Li Luomin (Freestyle) Time: 2 minutes, 25.8 seconds

(Guangdong Team) Su Tianmo (Backstroke) Guo Zhenheng (Breaststroke) Chen Qisong (Sidestroke)

Ren Mengxiong (Freestyle) Time: 2 minutes, 30.4 seconds

Ou Enzhao's Breaststroke Creates a New Far East Record

The 200-meter breaststroke was held jointly for men and women. The focus was on whether Ou Enzhao could break the Far East record. Yang Xiuzhen also joined as a pace swimmer, but using the freestyle. On the men's side were Fang Zongyu from Hong Kong, Guo Zhenheng and Wang Yaomin from Guangdong. Within 50 meters, Wang and Fang were in the lead, with Guo second. Ou and Yang were side by side in the rear, but less than a foot apart. After the turn, Fang was four or five feet ahead. Little Guo steadily closed the gap, but without effect. Xiuzhen, as always, did her own thing, approaching little Guo and keeping pace with him. Ou, due to her small stature, was still a foot behind. In the third leg, Fang gradually pulled away. Xiuzhen closed in on Yaomin, while little Guo, due to excessive fatigue from the relay, did not try very hard, walking hand in hand with Ou Enzhao, even more intimately. In the fourth leg, Fang pushed forward, reaching the finish line twelve feet ahead. Wang Yaomin finished ahead of Xiuzhen by a hand, while Guo and Ou were more than ten feet behind. Ou achieved a time of 3 minutes, 52.2 seconds, breaking Chen Huanqiong's Far East record of 3 minutes, 58 seconds, but not breaking Xiuqiong's national record of 3 minutes, 41 seconds, because the national standard is higher than the Far East standard. On the men's side, because they were pace swimmers, their scores were not counted.

Ou Enzhao 3 minutes, 52.2 seconds (Breaks Far East Record)

Three Performances are Miraculously Skilled

Yesterday's newly added programs included Chen Zhenxing and Zeng Hefu's butterfly stroke performance, with a distance of 50 meters. Zhenxing took the lead by one foot, timed exactly at 36 seconds flat. After the four-stroke relay, Chen Zhenxing also performed a 50-meter underwater swim, unofficially timed at 36.6 seconds. Underwater swimming cannot be done without real skill. It requires completing the entire length in one breath and being agile. The announcer specially explained this during Zhenxing's performance to show encouragement. Finally, Huang Xihan and Su Tianmo, the diving kings from the South, performed high board diving, including swallow style, sickle style, back bend style, half-turn entry style, backward somersault entry style, and synchronized double entry style, either like swallows skimming the water, tired birds returning to the forest, dragons soaring, or tigers leaping, with waves splashing and cheers erupting. Among them, the synchronized double entry style was the most popular with the audience. Such performances cannot be achieved without being proficient in this art, truly miraculously skilled.

Shanghai-Guangdong United Team Wins Water Polo Match

The most interesting water polo match was held after all the other events. The referee was Mr. Ye Guanyan. At the sound of the silver whistle, the athletes of both teams leaped forward. Zhang Rongguang, the forward of the Shanghai-Guangdong United Team, took the lead, carrying the ball straight ahead, invincible. Chen Fuxing, the defender of the Hong Kong-Malaya United Team, was unable to stop him. Rongguang swung the ball, hitting the target directly, less than a minute after the start of the match. At the center line kickoff, Shanghai got the ball again, passing it to the right forward Shi Jinpei, who passed it to Guo Zhenheng. After many passes, the ball returned to Shi's hand, and he scored again three feet from the goal. After the kickoff, Guo "Frog King," the center back, personally led the charge, heading to the front line to capture the flag, but the long-range shot missed. He advanced again and scored another goal. The Hong Kong-Malaya team suffered repeated losses. Although General Chen Ziqing was in the center, the team lacked fighting spirit, and their defenses were wide open. Chen Qisong charged forward and scored again. In a blink of an eye, the first half ended, with the Shanghai-Guangdong United Team leading 4-0. In the second half, both sides only played for one minute, feeling the water was too cold, and the game ended without a clear winner. The final score was 4-0, with the Shanghai-Guangdong team winning decisively. Overall, the Hong Kong-Malaya team's forwards also had many dangerous attacks on the goal, but they were all saved by Huang Jizhou and Zhou Yuanyun, the defenders and goalkeeper of the Shanghai-Guangdong team. The performances were wonderful, and there was much applause. The lineups are as follows:

Lianglu Bureau Hosts Yacht and Tennis Competitions, Held at the Garden Hotel on the 26th and 27th of This Month

The Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Lianglu Railway Bureau in this city, in order to promote sports, enhance national health, and encourage interest in travel, will specifically hold two amateur competitions, Qingyang Port yachting and tennis, on the 26th and 27th of this month at the Qingyang Port Railway Garden Hotel. If you want to register to participate and ask questions, please contact the Passenger Transport Section, Business Department of the North Station Transportation Office. The methods are as follows:

(A) Yacht Race

(1) Qualification: Any adult amateur athlete in Shanghai with considerable experience in water sports can participate. (2) Organization: Participants are divided into male and female groups. (3) Quota: Three people form a team. Men's and women's groups compete separately. Each group must have at least three teams to start the competition, but the total number of teams in both groups is limited to 40. (4) Referees: The bureau hires sports experts to serve as referees. (5) Selection: In this competition, each group selects the three teams with the best results. (6) All participants will be given a commemorative badge as a souvenir. The members of each winning team will each be given a separate prize. (7) Registration: When registering, three people form a team. If one person in each team is absent, the remaining two cannot participate, but they can still enjoy the benefits according to the regulations.

(B) Tennis Competition

(1) Qualification: Any amateur athlete in Shanghai (except those who have represented in international competitions) can participate. (2) Organization: Divided into men's and women's groups, each group is divided into singles and doubles. (3) Quota: Singles are based on one person, and doubles are based on two people. Each unit is regarded as a team. The number of singles and doubles teams in both groups must each be at least three, and at most ten. (4) Equipment: Rackets are prepared by the participants themselves, and tennis balls are provided by the bureau. (5) Referees: The bureau hires tennis experts to serve as referees. (6) Selection: The two best players in singles and doubles in both groups will be selected. (7) Awards: All participants will be given a commemorative badge as a souvenir. The members of the winning team will each be given a separate prize.

Farewell Moment (Photo by Ye Changlie)

All-China Games Archery Referee Zhang Weizhong Discusses Archery and its Promotion, Archery Possesses the Great Brave National Spirit, Public Performance at Daxia University This Afternoon

Archery, originally a good sport for physical training in our country, was specially added to the All-China Games last year to arouse public interest in archery. Yesterday, a reporter from the Guoguang News Agency met with Zhang Weizhong, the archery referee of this All-China Games. It is said that archery is of great benefit to education, military affairs, culture, and the promotion of national spirit. Mr. Zhang was also invited by Daxia University in this city and will hold a public performance at the school today. The details are recorded as follows:

Cultivate Perseverance and Decisiveness

According to Zhang Weizhong, archery in education can activate muscles and bones, strengthen muscles, exercise the spirit, and cultivate temperament, so as to cultivate the virtues of observing discipline, advocating cooperation, perseverance, decisiveness, and integrity. It can also educate rationality and exercise thinking. In the use of intelligence, it can gradually cultivate calm and precise observation, and correct and rapid judgment. Moreover, recreational archery can regulate laborious and tired life. As for military affairs, archery is actually the basic practice of shooting.

Promote the Brave National Spirit

Furthermore, the relationship with our country's culture and national spirit is even more important. Archery was originally one of the six arts in our country, and it is also a culture of peace, possessing a great brave national spirit. At the same time, it can recall the glorious history of our Chinese nation, which has coexisted with bows and arrows for four thousand years. In other words, the existence of bows and arrows is the existence of the glorious history of China.

Shoot for One Hour a Day, Can be Completed in Half a Month

As for the promotion method, in groups, classes can be set up for group practice. Archery for one hour a day, and archery theory for one hour. It can be learned in ten days, and then gradually practice, and advance to intermediate and advanced shooting methods. For individuals, I have written a book "Outline of Bow and Arrow Studies", which can be consulted for practice.

Public Performance This Afternoon

Mr. Zhang was also invited by Daxia University in this city yesterday, and will hold a public performance at the school at 4:00 PM this afternoon. Performance items: (1) 40-meter No. 1 rectangular target, (2) 20-meter No. 4 circular target, (3) 20-meter No. 6 rectangular target, (4) Shooting apples, (5) Moving target in the upward direction.

The Sixth National Woodcut Joint Exhibition Closes, Will Move to Beijing, Guangdong and Other Places for Continued Exhibition, Good Results Achieved During the Ten-Day Exhibition in Shanghai

The Sixth National Woodcut Joint Exhibition has been exhibited at the Shanghai Chinese Art and Culture Society since the Double Ten Festival. It closed yesterday after ten days. It will be transferred to Nanjing, Guangzhou and other places immediately. Regarding the achievements of this exhibition in Shanghai, the works are rich and the content is wonderful, which is an unprecedented initiative in Shanghai. During the exhibition period, more than 100,000 spectators, Luo Qingzhen's "Going Upstream", Li Hua's "Angry Horse", Lan Jia's "Yellow Train Fire", Yefu's "Funeral" and other works are finely crafted and ingenious, and they all expressed their admiration. In addition, Yefu invented two brick carvings, which combine the preciousness of ancient wood carvings and the splendor of oriental art. In addition, there are hundreds of folk New Year paintings, which are collected from the north and south and represent the customs and preferences of various places, which are also valuable works.

Little Men (71)

— Originally Written by Ms. Alcott of the United States, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"Oh, don't say that!" Mrs. Pei said busily, "I have loved this very thing since I had this large group of children, I have been the happiest. You know, Fuli Zi, I have deep sympathy for Nan'en, because I was such a naughty child at the time, so I know everything. She is full of energy, as long as you teach her how to use these energies, she can be as good as Xiaomei. According to her intelligence and agility, she must also like homework. If we can properly guide her, then a little bug that plays all day long may soon become a busy and happy child. I know how to discipline her, because I remember how my beloved late mother disciplined, and also the end　"

"Yes, since her mother died, she has been lawless at home. She is such a smart child. It would be a pity if she were spoiled by the servants. I have been paying attention to her for quite some time. That day I met her father in town, I asked him why he didn't send her to school. He said he was also willing, if he could find a girls' school that was as good as our boys' school. Therefore, I know he will be happy to send her here; why don't we drive over to his place this afternoon to see what his opinion is?"

"Aren't you worried enough, my Shu, but you still want to bring in a little sprite?" Mr. Pei said, patting the hand placed on his shoulder.

Finance: Although the Rumor of Indian Silver Rose Sharply, the Gold Standard Was Weak Before Becoming Strong

Rumors of Reducing Silver Import Tax and Increasing Gold Export Tax in India; Once Broke Through the 50 Yuan Mark, Resulting in a Rise of 6.6 Yuan

Yesterday, the gold market was erratic and easily stimulated. Major players had different demands. However, due to rumors of India reducing silver import tax and increasing gold export tax, although Indian silver rose, it was still surrounded by buying interest. In the early morning, with the overseas silver market rising in London and stable in the US, the forward silver price in Monte Carlo was unchanged or slightly reduced. Exchange rates rose uniformly. London gold rose four pence, and sentiment was stable. Off-site pre-market trading opened at 43.4 yuan. Yongli, Chunyuan, Yongda, Decheng, and Xie Da Xiang all advanced, rising to 46.7 yuan. Fuxing, Yonghui, Xiang Wanfeng supplied at high prices, retreating to 5 yuan. The morning opened high. After the opening, the central bank's listing was announced, with the English market stable and the American market rising. Customs gold unit rose three percent, and the standard gold price was listed at 947.5 yuan. Sentiment was still stable, and buyers took the opportunity to move, and a step-by-step increase was reported, almost approaching the 50 yuan mark. Banks took the opportunity to sell, blocking the rise. The HSBC bank listed the English and American markets as stable, still having some rotation. Later, the banks' selling appetite was sensitive, and they sold off one after another, stimulating selling pressure, and falling step by step, once turning weak. However, buyers maintained at low prices, and the exchange rate was still stable, gradually improving. Banks sold US dollars, and buyers divested somewhat, gradually moving downstream. However, the situation was very mediocre. Predicting the situation of Indian "small two annas," at noon, the supply and demand sides seemed quite balanced, and the banks were also unwilling to excessively sell. The market was stable. Banks mutually traded, the market situation was volatile, and buying interest was relatively strong, making it easy to pull up. Unexpectedly, the first telegram from India reported a rise of twenty-five annas, and selling pressure was enthusiastic for a while, suddenly falling. However, a part of the psychology was based on the fact that no telegram was received for spot goods, and the telegram noted that it needed to be investigated, expressing doubt. Therefore, there was a lot of maintenance after the low, and large households rushed to buy. It was said that India reduced the import tax on silver, but at the same time increased the export tax on gold, and sentiment turned positive, and buying interest was extremely strong, lacking supply, and broke through the 50 yuan mark, rising rapidly, and the situation was very positive. Grain: Foreign Wheat Price Drop Sweeps Through Flour and Wheat Markets

After the flour market opened, near- and far-month contracts fell sharply across the board. The price drop was very severe. The far-month contracts once fell by about 5 cents. This was largely because international conditions eased, foreign wheat was widely reported to be falling, and spot foreign wheat was actively being offered for sale. The market was greatly shaken. New buyers remained on the sidelines, and hoarders sought to unload their holdings. The market followed suit and plummeted. Moreover, several factories were actively selling off their holdings, making it difficult to rally the market in the short term. The near-month contracts were relatively stable due to demand for spot goods from the Northern Gang.
