Oil Market: New Asphalt Already Has Market Demand

New asphalt is about to arrive. However, since Hubei and other provinces are located thousands of miles away, new oil typically arrives in Shanghai at the end of the eleventh lunar month. Therefore, the local firms and candle makers have relied on the neighboring province of Zhejiang for their supply. The abundance or scarcity of the annual harvest in the asphalt-producing areas of eastern and western Zhejiang is of particular concern to asphalt firms and candle makers in Shanghai. According to reports, this year's harvest in Zhejiang is generally abundant. The fruits borne by the asphalt trees are more plentiful than in previous years, even without increased cultivation efforts, which is unprecedented. However, the presses in the asphalt-producing areas of eastern Zhejiang press both tung oil and asphalt oil. Since the tung oil production season is one month earlier than asphalt oil, and tung oil prices are currently high, the presses are prioritizing the pressing of tung oil. Although the asphalt oil production season has arrived, it will inevitably be pushed back by tung oil. Therefore, the initial supply may not be abundant. However, the Jiaxing area in western Zhejiang, which does not produce tung oil, can be expected to begin pressing on schedule, likely in the first ten days of the eleventh lunar month. It is currently heard that some people from inland areas have come to Shanghai to sell asphalt, with prices totaling 16.40 to 16.50 yuan per picul delivered, which is cheaper than Jing asphalt oil. Therefore, buyers are very enthusiastic.

Free Talk

Natural Description (Part 1)

— Qu Yi

In literary works, natural description has always been regarded as very important. The ancients said, "Mountains and forests are in decline, the mansion of literary thought," which is what this means. But why must there be natural description in literary works? The reason for that has also been said long ago:

"The seasons alternate, yin and yang alternately prevail; the movement of things affects the heart. When the yang energy sprouts, the colt steps forward; when the yin law congeals, the red crow is ashamed. Even the smallest insects are affected, so profound is the influence of the four seasons. When jade emits its brilliance and talents reveal their pure energy, who can remain at peace? Therefore, the beginning of spring brings joy; the torrential summer brings melancholy; the clear air of autumn inspires lofty ambitions; the boundless snow evokes solemn thoughts. Each season has its own characteristics, and each thing has its own appearance. Emotions change with things, and words express those emotions. Even a single leaf can welcome intention, and the sound of an insect can draw the heart. How much more so when the clear wind and bright moon share the night, and the white sun and spring forest share the morning! Therefore, poets are endlessly inspired by things, associating them without end. Wandering among the myriad phenomena, dwelling in the realm of sight and sound, they attempt to depict their appearance, following the objects in their twists and turns. Attaching words to sounds, they also linger with the heart..."

This is to say that people live in nature and are constantly affected by it. Literature is the expression of people's emotions; therefore, natural description is unavoidable. But there are two points worth noting here. The first is the relationship between man and nature. The second is the method of natural description. Throughout history, the attitude of men toward nature and the method of expression have been almost the same.

The relationship between man and nature has probably gone through several stages. Initially, it was one of ignorance and harmony with nature: one of submission to nature. Then, with the invention of drilling for fire and building nests of wood, people learned to utilize nature and overcome it. But since the tools became increasingly advanced, people knew how to further create nature. Originally, human happiness should be built on creating nature. The ultimate purpose of human history is to call people to the goal of struggling with nature. But the literati of the past were all unproductive parasites, so they could not only fail to unleash the power of overcoming nature and creating nature, but they also could not discover such power in themselves—in human abilities. Therefore, the literati became the weakest of all people; Huang Zhongze's poem: "Immortals and Buddhas are both unachieved, only knowing how to lament alone at night; wind-driven sails are full of sad songs, willow catkins bring a bad reputation; nine out of ten people deserve a white eye, a scholar is useless in everything; do not let poems cause worry and recognition, spring birds and autumn insects make their own sounds," can be said to have written about the literati's incompetence. In particular, comparing literati to spring birds and autumn insects is undoubtedly appropriate.

Poets never dare to fight back against the attacks of nature, and they cannot fight back. Therefore, even the sound of curses is not heard. Nature is infinitely great and mysterious in front of poets. Nature is God. Originally, in the era of natural economy, although farmers could utilize nature, partially overcome nature, and change nature, when nature exerted its greatest power (such as storms and droughts), they could only sigh in their homes and do nothing about it. It is not surprising that fetishism exists in peasant society. Qu Yuan's Nine Songs are said to be folk songs used to worship gods in the State of Chu, but they have been passed down after being polished by Qu Yuan. The overall impression of the Nine Songs is all about praising the spirituality and mystery of nature. It has a strong undertone of fetishism. For example, in Mountain Spirit, it says: "There seems to be someone on the mountain, draped in ivy and wearing dodder. She seems to be glaring, then she seems to smile. She admires me for my graceful form. She rides a red leopard, followed by a patterned civet. Her carriage is made of magnolia, and her flag is tied with cinnamon. She lives among rocks and wears sweetgrass. She breaks off fragrant stems and leaves them for her beloved." Also, in Lesser Master of Fate, it says: "Wearing lotus clothes and a belt of sweet herbs, she comes and goes in a flash. She spends the night on the Emperor's plains, who is she waiting for at the edge of the clouds? I will travel with you on the Nine Rivers, where the rushing wind rises and the water waves. I will bathe with you in Xianchi, and dry your hair in the Yang River." Also, in Lady Xiang, it says: "I heard that the beautiful woman is summoning me, and I will ride with her. She builds a house in the water, thatched with lotus leaves. The walls are fragrant with purple sandalwood, and the hall is strewn with fragrant peppers. The pillars are cinnamon and chinaberry, the lintels are magnolia, and the rooms are filled with medicine. She weaves dodder into curtains and spreads sweet herbs. White jade is used as weights, and rocks and orchids are used for fragrance. The house is thatched with sweetgrass and lotus leaves, and surrounded by Northern Hyacinth. All kinds of herbs are planted in the courtyard, and fragrant herbs are built into the gate. The nine melodies are played together, welcoming her arrival like clouds." These are all extreme efforts to sculpt the gods and greatness of nature, and to gather the most beautiful things in the universe to describe the nobility and fragrance of nature's personality. At its root, there is a strong fetishistic thought.

People feel the insignificance of their own abilities in the face of nature. Thus, the idea of worshiping nature arose. As a result of worshiping nature, they want to learn from nature in order to seek its vastness. The Taoist idea of returning to simplicity has its roots here. But the vastness sought by Taoism is only a kind of spiritual victory, not actual vastness. They want to break away from the human world, follow the "laws of nature," and live alone in this nature, existing forever with nature. Whether they can live on or not is a question. But people call these kinds of people gods or immortals. Perhaps some of them cannot live on and quietly starve to death. But some people call them immortals. And some people write poems to praise them and admire them; the poem says:

"The kingfisher plays with the orchid shoots, the colors of the guest and the scene are even more brilliant. Green vines bind the tall forest, covering a mountain in mist. In the midst is a silent hermit, quietly whistling and playing a clear stringed instrument. He releases his emotions beyond the heavens, chewing herbs and drinking from flying springs. Red Pine roams above, riding a swan in purple smoke. He pulls at Floating Hill's sleeve on the left and claps Hongya's shoulder on the right. May I ask you, ephemeral beings, how can you know the years of the tortoise and crane? How can the six dragons be stopped? The flow of fortune changes. When the times interact, people think of home, and autumn is longing for summer. The Huaihai River turns into a tiny bird, but my life alone does not transform. Although I want to surpass Danxi, I cannot ride the clouds and dragons. Ashamed of lacking the virtue of Lu Yang, I turn the sun back to three houses. Facing the river, I grieve for old age, and I touch my heart in solitary sadness." (Guo Han's Poem on Traveling as an Immortal)

Stream Bathing

— Yao Mu

I really like water. A small stream, a pool, all evoke an unnamed joy in me, especially when I encounter a gurgling stream or a splashing pool in the mountains. It is as if I were hearing the free-spirited sound of the seven-stringed zither in the silent night, or seeing the faint smile of the twin whirlpools before a solemn goddess. I am particularly fascinated.

I remember that the first time I traveled as a child was to Mount Dinghu, which is famous for its Flying Water Pool. The emerald green pool water, the cascading long waterfalls, and the tall trees brushing against each other still linger in my heart. Like the fluff of first love, I really idealized the secluded interest of mountain springs.

This year, there is a beautiful Yellow Dragon Pool waterfall near our mountain residence. I have been there twice, but unfortunately not after it rained and the springs were flowing. But sitting on a sheep-fat-like stone beach, watching the clear, cold spring flow out from between the chaotic rocks and trees, winding and meandering between the stones and rock holes, the sound of water filled my ears. Dipping my feet into the water and washing my face with water, the heat and fatigue were all dissipated by the ice-cold pleasure. Looking down from the Wan Shou Bridge, I saw a waterfall falling from the top of the mountain, like silver silk and ice chips, cascading for tens of feet and condensing into an ancient jade-like blue pool. The stone walls on both sides were steep, and there were traces of flowing springs. I could imagine the spectacular sight of thousands of valleys flowing after a heavy rain. The walls were covered with green moss, and small trees with vines growing on them, and grasses like orchids and iris. Sprinkled with splashing water flowers, they were fresh and dripping. Several golden daylilies were hidden in the grass and trees, showing off their charm. In addition to the glittering water and springs, there was the fragrance of grass and flowers. Being in it, it felt like sipping a thousand-year-old mellow wine, forgetting both myself and the outside world, and like ascending to a pure land, where not a speck of dust could touch my body or mind.

We also once moved in the mountains. There was a mountain stream a mile away from our new residence, where cold springs gushed out, and chaotic rocks piled up. The scenery was so quiet and secluded that it resembled the scenes in Liu Zongyuan's short essays. When we passed by, we already felt that it was a good place to take a bath. The day after arriving, at noon, I took Lao Zhang and our bathing equipment and clothes to be washed there. After passing a few houses, we followed a small path buried in lush grass, turned a few bends, and heard the tinkling sound of the spring. Following the sound of the water, we walked down a few more steps and saw the mountain stream.

It hadn't rained for a few days after, so the stream was still not small. The rocks varied in size and were scattered in a crisscross pattern. Depending on the shape of the rocks, some places swirled and surged, some places formed small pools, and some places gushed like small waterfalls. Pear trees and some unknown large-leaved trees were planted diagonally on both sides of the stream, their branches and leaves crisscrossing and forming a natural pergola, even shading the stream. The high sun peered through the gaps in the branches and leaves, and round shadows swayed in the pool. Depending on the depth of the water and the brightness of the sunlight, the water presented various colors, such as cyan, light green, light yellow, and snow white, but they were all equally clear, pure and ice-cold.

Two young girls had arrived before us and were squatting by the stream washing clothes. We took off our boots and, with clumsy movements, jumped from one rock to another, from low places to high places, surveying the surroundings of the stream. Then, we washed the clothes we brought in a hurry and hung them on sunny rocks to dry. After the girls left, we chose a deeper and more open place for our bathing place. The water was just over our knees. When we first dipped our feet, we felt a chill all over our bodies, and we were about to shiver. After rubbing for a while, we felt better. Sometimes I lay in the water with my whole body, sometimes I lay on my back and let the flowing spring water wash over me, and sometimes I sat on a rock and splashed water with my feet. Half the time I was bathing, half the time I was playing. I didn't know where the boring feeling of having nothing to do all day had disappeared to!

After bathing in the stream, we chose a boulder like a bed to lie down on and sunbathe. The sunlight suddenly stopped, and the rain followed the cool breeze. The rustling sound of rain hitting the leaves and the gurgling sound of the spring echoed each other. We put on our clothes and hid under the dense leaves. After a while, the rain stopped, and the sun came out again. The mountain stream, after being bathed in rain, was even more green and moist.

I have also taken various kinds of baths. Needless to say, a stuffy steam bath – if you allow me to use a woman as a metaphor – a hot spring bath is like an affectionate wife, a sea bath is like a beautiful and graceful young woman, while a stream bath has the style of "Wearing a green sleeve in the cold, leaning on slender bamboo at sunset." Those who have tried stream bathing will not consider this metaphor an exaggeration, right?

Those few days were when the moon was bright. The mountain stream under the moon must have been very quiet and secluded. I imagined that the night was as cool as water, the rocks were as cool as ice, the trees were crooked and slanting, and the silver light was shimmering. There was a sound of flowing water. The water nymphs and goddesses who are said to bathe in secret in mythology, if they really exist, must also be bathing here at this time! Unfortunately, I was busy for the next three days after the bath, and I didn't step into the moonlight to seek that dreamlike scene. I still regret this even now!

Two Kinds of Fathers

— Mo Fu

Balzac, the French writer, has a novel called "Old Goriot." It begins like this: "Old Goriot, a man who had made a fortune, loved his two daughters very much. In order to marry them off in great splendor, he spared no expense in giving them all his possessions. He himself ended up living in poverty in a student boarding house, afraid to visit them for fear of embarrassing them. Later, he became very ill, and only a young man living in the same boarding house took care of him. The young man saw that the old man was getting worse and quickly asked the boarding house servant to notify his two daughters to come and see him; however, the messenger returned alone." Until Old Goriot breathed his last, the young man who was caring for him had personally gone to invite his two daughters, but they never came. On Old Goriot's side, he kept muttering and rambling, "...If I were still a rich man, still holding onto my property, and hadn't given it all to them, they would definitely come, they would frequently kiss my cheeks!...With money, they would be visible...They have hearts of stone...I loved them too much, so they treat me this way. A father should always be a rich old man...Daughters! Arlette, Delphine (the names of his daughters)! I want to see them. Call the police to arrest them...Justice help me! Heaven's law, national law...should all help me...A father trampled under the feet of his children..." These words seemed very clear and rational, but he was still planning how—"to go to Odessa to sell noodles...to earn millions of silver...Let them come, even if it's for the money, I'm willing to be deceived by them..." Finally, he shouted, "Even touching the hem of their clothes would be good...Just want to touch the hem of their clothes...and I would be content...I bless them...bless..." And so he died. Blessing such daughters even at his death, it can truly be said that his love for his daughters reached its extreme.

Perhaps some would think this depiction is a bit excessive, that such daughters could not possibly exist. True, this is indeed not very common, and to some, it may seem cruel. However, if we think about it, things like this seem to be encountered everywhere, and having encountered them, one feels that he hasn't written enough, that they haven't even plotted to murder their father for his property. The world is truly full of children more ruthless than these! Of course, we don't have to respect our parents to the point of unreasonable and absolute obedience, but to ignore them when they have no money, or to secretly plot to murder them for their wealth, is indeed contrary to human nature.

This is a kind of father who dotes on his children, disregarding his own life and death. Fathers like Old Goriot are really not special; most parents dote on their children. What's special is only in these two daughters.

Because of this novel, it reminded me of another kind of father who is completely different from this. Several years ago, I lived in a small city. My landlord was a retired soldier around forty years old. He only had one child. In the past, his family finances were not bad, but because he had nothing to do, he developed a gambling habit, and soon squandered his entire fortune. However, he was not worried about the loss of his property, but worried only when the last residence was sold off, and his wife, four months pregnant, miscarried from the shock. Since then, she had four miscarriages in seven or eight years, unable to hold onto the fetus. He always advocated "one more son, one more happiness," so he naturally wouldn't fail to cherish his only son. However, his method of loving his son was completely different from Old Goriot's—in daily life, he would enjoy better food and clothing himself, leaving his child to watch with longing from the side. He had a reason to defend himself—the child will have plenty of time to eat and wear good things! Not only that, but his family education was frighteningly strict. Even though he was only a few years old, the child had to obey absolutely, just like he treated soldiers, without any reason. As a result, the child was crushed under his heavy pressure. He was listless all day long, always looking like his soul had left his body, almost like a fool. Moreover, his love was different from Old Goriot's—Old Goriot's love was pure, entirely based on blood ties, without any purpose. But this other person was the opposite, with a purpose—hoping to enjoy the happiness bestowed by his son in the future, so he spared no effort in harsh training,鞭撻孩子猛進 (?), hoping to achieve his own purpose, disregarding the child's own welfare. We won't worry about the results for now. This kind of fatherly love that contains other purposes is really more cruel and inappropriate than the two daughters' treatment of Old Goriot. However, such fathers are as common in today's society as Old Goriots, and can be encountered anytime, anywhere.

Dog Racing Track

— Da Bao

In the sky are azure clouds,

On the ground is a pale green lawn.

Stars are shining in the clouds,

Mysterious lights are flashing on the grassland.

This is a paradise on earth,

This is a world of entertainment.

Indeed, every night, thousands of visitors come here to have fun.

Greyhounds wearing red vests are racing with all their might,

Ladies and gentlemen are cheering and applauding wildly.

They need to use rowdiness and shouting,

To compensate for the fatigue of their lives.

The human beings of the end of the century,

Let time pass like this:

Rowdiness, boredom,

Until they make fun of animals.

Regardless of whether the world becomes a doghouse,

Everyone cheers for the fall of happiness:

Pity the wisdom of mankind,

Sold cheaply to this kind of human civilization.

Honorable Old Woman (12)

— Written by Ekuma Shū, Translated by Ren Jun

One late autumn night, a violent knocking suddenly echoed at my door. Unexpectedly, the knocker turned out to be from the police station. It turned out that the old woman had just been found hanging herself in the courtyard of a temple on the edge of the city, and the police were there to notify us.

The people in my house were all shocked. Because on this day, the old woman had still come to my house early in the morning and worked until night before going back.

"Oh, so she really went crazy. Lately, I always felt she was a bit funny... But because the old woman was funny to begin with, I didn't pay much attention..."

My mother said this and began to chant Buddhist scriptures.

The accountant and the male servant ran out. I also quietly followed them, because I wanted to see something scary. It was a dark and cold night. Countless small stars in the sky were twinkling. We relied on the light of the lanterns and hurried towards the dark edge of the city.

When we arrived at the temple, the old woman's body had already been taken down and placed on a mat under the steps of the main hall, covered with another mat.

A policeman and two other people were constantly shining the light of an electric lamp into the darkness, illuminating the lump under the mat.

I was both flustered and scared. Curled up in a ball, hiding behind the accountant. After listening to the people at the scene recounting the discovery, he went to the corpse in silence. Then, he quietly pulled back the mat, and I peeked out from behind him, trembling.

The shocking thing was that the old woman was still wearing that tattered 四 (?), and the 章 (?) on her chest was shining.

I suddenly felt like I heard her crazy voice:

"This is honor! This is honor!" (The End)

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Random Talk

Roosevelt's Son Punished

— Jia Wei

Every morning, I turn to the first couple of pages of this newspaper, which, as usual, are filled with new information about the Abyssinian question: "Ten thousand Abyssinian troops prepare on the Ogeden line, the East African War is about to begin," "Sixteen thousand Italian troops continue to head to East Africa," "League of Nations sanctions are not relaxed," "Britain replies to the French government, the Mediterranean fleet is difficult to withdraw," "Britain may blockade the Italian coast..." Thinking of those Italian troops, who are known as "civilized people," and of their leader Mussolini—the second Lincoln, he prides himself?—wanting to "conquer" those Abyssinians, who are regarded as "barbarians," and innocent women and children, so bravely" using gas and dumdum bullets to carry out massacres, in the reader's feeling, even the spaces between the words on the newspaper page seemed filled with the atmosphere of gunpowder, poison gas, and blood.

However, in another corner of today's newspaper, on the other side of these bloody messages, we also read a record of "yellow journalism." The content is copied as follows:

"President Roosevelt's son was fined five dollars today by Judge Pancost for speeding. Roosevelt's son is currently a junior at Harvard University. On September 18, he was driving at 65 miles per hour" (National News Agency Dispatch on September 18).

"Speeding, a fine of five dollars," this was originally a commonplace thing, but the news agency had to make a special dispatch for it; and the newspaper editor added "flair" to it and published it to attract attention. Of course, this is because the person involved is the son of the current US President Roosevelt, right?

Originally, as the author himself, there is no need to create a personal biography for him. However, putting aside those gunpowder-filled news items that I read every day and thinking quietly, I feel that there are a few words to say.

The law, originally, is the "superstructure of society." It is the norm of every society, that is, the standard for individual behavior, regardless of status or class. It is precisely "honesty above and below, treating everyone equally." However, precisely because all the superstructures of society have to change with the changes in the economic base of society, the law cannot be an exception. But throughout history, society has been an unequal society. In this way, the law has become a tool used by the rulers to oppress the lower masses, which has become an undisguisable fact.

Therefore, Roosevelt's son breaking the law and being fined is such an ordinary little thing, and it has to be telegraphed and published in newspapers around the world. Apart from its exaggeration and propaganda components, under certain conditions, it is worthy of people's attention. Especially today, under the state of social psychology in our society, which only cares about power and profit.

However, to say it again, we think that it is not enough to rely solely on this to maintain the dignity of existing laws and to demonstrate the equality of society. You must know that under certain circumstances, the rulers are using this method to whitewash their true faces. Therefore, if we want society to be peaceful and bright, and if we want the law to be equal, then we must first equalize the social foundation on which our laws and other superstructures depend!

Page 16

Book Strap

— Yan

The dismissal bell rang for the third class. Liu Fugao winked at his companions. As the class monitor, he stood up and shouted loudly, "One, two, three." After the teacher stepped out of the classroom with his books, the classroom became chaotic, like a beehive that had been overturned. Everyone called out to their close friends, arranging to walk together, or to go somewhere else to play. Wrapping books, knocking on desks, throwing rubber balls, everything was making noise. Naturally, there were also a few refined fellows who had a beautiful book strap; this strap had caused envy in the classroom. With a stack of books, they would buckle it this way and that, and then carry it steadily in their hands. When walking, holding the end of the strap, the stack of books would sway back and forth, and with the sound of their little leather shoes, the appearance was pretty enough. But buckling this strap takes a little time, and the knot must be buckled in the very center of the stack of books, otherwise, when walking, it will bump against their knees. Liu Fugao was the class monitor, and the school awarded him a strap. He naturally happily went home to boast in front of his parents, and he could sway back and forth in front of his classmates. His closest friend and classmate, Wang Yuande, didn't have one, and he was very envious of Liu Fugao's book strap. For several days after school, he slipped away alone. Liu Fugao knew this, and he comforted him, saying that the school was biased, and that Wang Yuande's studies were also very good, his essays were always above 80 points, and he should also be awarded a book strap. But empty words didn't make Wang Yuande happy. When the two of them walked home together, he seemed not to want to be seen, walking close to the wall. For the last three days, Liu Fugao couldn't find Wang Yuande when school ended. The class monitor understood in his heart that he didn't bring his book strap to sway around today. He pulled Wang Yuande and said, "Today we'll still walk together, I won't use the book strap?" And there's something good to see today.

So after Liu Fugao winked, Wang Yuande deliberately stacked and re-stacked his few thin books, tidied them up again and again, and slowly unfolded the newspaper, wrapping the books as if he were folding handicrafts. The other classmates all hopped and skipped away. A few refined fellows carefully buckled the book straps in the center, swaying and swaying out of the classroom. The two of them stuck out their tongues and, as in the past, held hands affectionately, going out of the school's back door. The school's back door was a real alley, and you had to walk another block to get around to the front door. But they often walked this way, they wanted to walk slowly, avoiding the eyes of their classmates, to go to a good place to see good things. It's not that Liu Fugao didn't want everyone to follow him to see it, because this thing was good to see, but it wasn't enough to speak out loud. He himself was the class monitor, and the class monitor couldn't be so sloppy and do the wrong thing. Wang Yuande was a good friend, so naturally he was an exception.

From the school's front door, crossing two more streets, there was a small movie theater. When they got out of school, it was just about time for the second show at 5:30 to begin. At the entrance, there was a square box playing nice-sounding songs. There were some that Liu Fugao and Wang Yuande could also sing, like "The Road," "Graduation Song," which were all taught at school. But the sound coming from that box was loud, as if many people were singing together. Near the door was a glass cabinet, which displayed still photos from the film. If they were just looking at this, they wouldn't have to be so secretive, because they were thinking about the movie that was playing inside. They came up with a method: secretly hiding by the door, and when three or five adults bought tickets to go in, they would immediately go in with them. The rule of this small movie theater was that every adult could bring one child. They had seen many movies using this method, but this method could not be known to their classmates. Liu Fugao was the class monitor!

Yesterday he didn't walk the same way with Wang Yuande again. He felt that this book strap had caused him to lose a good friend. He didn't know why, but he walked to the movie theater again. He saw that there were quite a few still photos in the glass cabinet, singles, doubles, photos of foreign women dancing. Liu Fugao originally wanted to use the old method to go in and take a look, but he wasn't very happy without Wang Yuande. He didn't bring the book strap today, to pull Wang Yuande to see the dancing.

But when they squeezed in behind three or five adults, they were stopped by the ticket taker, who said that children were not allowed. 一一鬧蹩扭, the people in front had already disappeared. They didn't understand the meaning of "children not allowed." The two of them discussed that the reason for being rejected was: this is foreign women dancing, you need to buy a ticket for each person, no children allowed. Then, they had to think of another method. Wang Yuande's idea was to save up their snack money for a few days. The class monitor seemed even smarter, he said to sell the book strap for money to watch the movie. In order to please his friend, he was willing to give up that swaying, pretty appearance. Wang Yuande was naturally even happier. They stood by the glass cabinet reluctantly, until the square box stopped singing, and then they walked along the way, thinking about the method of exchanging the book strap for money.

Scenery of Bali

— Cong Long

This Bali, known as the "Greece of the Tropics," certainly has many places worth remembering, praising, and lingering in.

Except for the high mountains in the west, the rest is a fertile plain suitable for planting. Even the high mountains, the grandeur and majesty of the caves, the solemnity and tranquility of the volcanic crater area, and the swirling and slowly moving clouds and mist at dawn and dusk, floating like jade belts among the sharp peaks, all these beautiful scenery can make people feel happy and broad-minded.

Bali's fertile land and the accessibility of its rivers, which are convenient for irrigation, mean that the rice fields are absolutely unaffected by disasters. Moreover, their planting is not limited by the seasons, and they can harvest and sow at any time. Whenever the weather is clear, walking in the suburbs, you can see many dark-skinned natives dotted in a vast expanse of paddy fields: some are busy transplanting rice seedlings, some are driving white buffaloes to plow the soil, and some are harvesting golden rice ears, all happily doing various tasks at different stages at the same time. Because of the mild climate, the fertility of the land, and the ease of planting, the economic situation of most Balinese people is prosperous.

Balinese women all completely expose their upper bodies, letting their pointed, towering breasts, like newly raised graves, tremble slightly with their steps. This is the case all year round, whether indoors or on the street. Men like to put red and white flowers in their hair. It is said that these are their customs, which have been popular from ancient times to the present. Whenever they bathe in the morning and evening, they all take a bath together in the river, men and women alike, completely naked, but it is rare to hear of irregular or lewd romantic behavior between the sexes. This group of beautiful human models in the clear water may make those who come here for the first time feel a little shy and disapproving.

They don't pay much attention to their houses, letting them be broken and rotten, dirty and narrow. They are in danger of collapsing in the face of storms, but they don't care and don't want to repair them, as if these are all small things that are not worth putting on their minds? They would rather spend a surprising amount of money on cockfights or temple fairs to worship the gods. Therefore, to see a complete and magnificent residence here (naturally referring to the general commoner class) is simply as rare as phoenix feathers and unicorn horns.

The Balinese all believe in religion, and worshiping the gods can be said to be one of their important daily tasks. They believe that everything on earth belongs to and is ruled by the gods, and that the gods can give people all happiness and good fortune. Therefore, in Bali, whether on high mountains, beaches, embankments, forests, villages, or outside every family's thatched hut and the palace, there are temples of all sizes. The only task of their梭巴 (village chief) is to build temples for the gods. Therefore, they compete with each other to improve the construction of the temples. Just looking at the carvings on the outer walls of the temple arches, the greatness of the project, and the excellence of the art, one cannot despise the Balinese.

Living in Bali, you can hear the sound of a low, deep bronze drum faintly wafting in the breeze every day, which is them holding a temple fair. When a temple fair is held, groups of women, wearing light and fluttering silk outer garments and adorned with gold and silver jewelry, walk in an orderly manner, row after row, snaking towards the temple, with all kinds of offerings on their heads, looking from a distance like a row of ornate carved Buddha statues in the Thousand Buddha Caves.

The Balinese are also good at dancing. Their dances often depict strange stories. The dancers wear golden helmets, carry daggers, and wear bright golden leaf outer garments. When dancing excitedly, these young dancing girls often draw out the daggers from their sides and cut open their chests, letting the bright red blood flow out and die. This is the same as when a plague occurs in the area, children dance around the hideous death god in front of the temple, and pierce their chests with the snake-shaped daggers in their hands. They believe that all happiness is given by the gods, and that dedicating oneself to the gods is a pure and noble thing!

Old Books

— Laborious Mind

When I am unbearably bored, I now like to settle myself in some quiet corner. Therefore, the old book stalls lined along the roadside have become my usual haunt. But one day, I discovered a miracle. Among a pile of old books, I saw two that caught my eye. I picked them up and looked at them closely—there was no mistake! It wasn’t my eyes deceiving me. These were the books of a friend who had fallen on hard times. I distinctly remembered a few jokingly scribbled words I had added to the copyright page, and a newspaper clipping tucked between pages one hundred and twenty-three. Nothing was wrong, everything was as it used to be, although the book had passed through countless hands. This book reminded me of life four months ago, when we were still chatting and laughing, still indulging in youthful games, happily enduring that series of painful and difficult days. At that time, no one would have imagined that things would turn out this way, especially me, becoming lonely and isolated in this vast city, enduring life's challenges without laughter. Thinking of this, I became even more attached to this old book.

"Boss, how much for this one?"

Although I knew very well that I didn't have a single copper coin in my pocket, I never gave up on the slightest glimmer of hope, because I knew this stall owner recognized me. Maybe I could ask him to hold it for me and come back to buy it in a few days. That's why I dared to inquire about the price.

"To be honest, we never exaggerate prices. If you want to buy it, it's eight dimes."

He replied in a tone that also seemed hopeful, because I knew there were times when his stall had virtually no business. After a moment, he added:

"And there are a few more here, all acquired together."

Then he flipped out five or six more. I recognized all five or six of these old books, and two of them were actually my own books that had ended up in his possession. Looking at these books, it was like seeing old friends, and I gazed at them affectionately. Although I was a little resentful that my friend had unfeelingly sold the books he had cherished for so many years, when I thought about his situation, I understood. He was so poor when he left this place, and if he hadn't sold these books, he would have been unable to survive. At the same time, I was willing to forgive him for not giving these books to his friends, because he no longer had that right. Nor could he borrow any money or receive any help from friends. Like me, I was the one who felt most sorry. I had promised him help, but I became a bounced check. I was also suffocating under the pressure of life. In the long period of being unemployed for half a year, I had tasted all of life's "enjoyments"...

"Want to buy?"

The owner, seeing me standing there lingering, looked at me strangely and impatiently.

"Ah, yes. I want to buy, but I really can't afford it today. Could you hold them for me? I'll come back to buy them as soon as I find the money, at most in a day or two."

I pleaded earnestly, and he grudgingly agreed.

But where could I find the money? When I hadn't even secured the rent, where could I find extra money to buy these books? So, I had no choice but to let the days pass one by one. Although my heart was anxiously empty, there was nothing I could do. Until one day, I borrowed a dollar, which was originally meant for food for the next few days, but I forgot everything and ran to the old book stall.

"Boss, the books?"

He gave an apologetic smile: "You haven't been here for more than a week. I thought you had forgotten about them, so I sold them all. Only this one is left."

This one was "A Woman and Society." I bought it at the lowest possible price. As I ate a bowl of plain noodles with the last of my money, I flipped through the book and smiled.

Storytelling

Zhu Xiaolin's Opening

New Voice (1380) 11:45 AM to 1:45 PM

Opening "Karmic Retribution Record Please Write"

Yulan is audacious and ruthless, unaware of treacherous schemes and major issues. After scaring Wang Tinggui to death, she escapes the net and flies away. She hides for a long time in a small boat, pretending to hire a village doctor. Who knows that without a hint of trouble, she is already at the South Building in the fifth or seventh term? Unaware of how she concealed it, she is very happy but also very suspicious. Returning home, she prepares gifts and visits to mourn, not mentioning the sudden death. Ashamed, she kowtows before the spirit tablet, her face flushed with embarrassment. The maid and mistress in mourning listen attentively, the voice and words are truly hers. She searched the garden several times but couldn't find her, hoping for a glimpse of her shadow over the wall. Tonight, a love letter is written in her own hand, showing that even with a broken lotus root, the thread remains. The letter is sent to Wang Wen, asking the maid to deliver it. Wang Lu hears the sound and knocks on the garden gate. The servant picks up the true evidence: a pile of flowers, a wall, and two steps. Who knows that the Dongren people planned to kill her, making it difficult to bear? The loyal maid and the loyal servant fear being deceived by the Liu family. They ask the official to investigate.

Cheng Fangzhou, Li Liansun, Mao Jiashu

Huamei (1060) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening "Yang Guifei's Birthday"

The sixth day of the sixth lunar month is hot. Songs and music are playing steadily in the Tang palace. Yang Guifei, especially favored in the Western Garden, feels resentment and self-pity. One misstep leads to eternal regret, foolish thoughts and infatuation entering the emotional demon. An Lushan's troops revolt in Fanyang, the road to Tongguan is not far. I fear, one general succeeds while ten thousand bones wither. The smoke of war rises, and the good people cry. How can we bear to be homeless and displaced? After thinking it over, I am finally a slave. I have no intention of going to the Hall of Eternal Life again, afraid of playing the pipa and the Dingchi harmony. I am afraid of entering the Huaqing Pool for a bath, afraid of scalding my tender skin. I have no intention of being a lotus flower growing on the same stem. It is better to sit by the window and teach the parrot. It is pleasing that the bird is more intelligent than the palace maids. First teach him three chapters of Qingping Tunes, then teach him the Great Compassion Mantra and recite Amitabha. Listen to him, the warbling sounds like a slave. Time passes quickly, making people old. May the heavens end the war soon. Guifei sighed lightly, her heart was in a mess. The emperor smiled and called out, "Ah Huan." Guifei is frightened. The birthday is on the first day of the sixth month, and the lychees are fresh and plentiful. The south sea offers tribute to the capital. The emperor and his ministers celebrate longevity in the Hall of Eternal Life. A small banquet is arranged for their enjoyment. May the loving couple live a loving life forever.

Xing Ruiting's Hairpin Phoenix

Huiling (1380) 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM

Opening "The Palace of Eternal Life"

In the Kaiyuan era, there was great peace, and orders were given to burn jewels and treasures. Song Zhang and Han were chosen to assist in governance, supporting the throne and aiding in the management of the country. One day, Emperor Tang was tired of eating and sleeping, and his dragon face was not happy after court. He summoned the court eunuch Gao Lishi, asking who was the beauty who could overturn a country. Since Taizhen was favored in the palace, a hairpin box was bestowed as a token of love. She received the king's new rain and dew, and bathed in the warm sun in spring. I see that she is exquisitely dressed, but her eyebrows do not let others. Sisters received favor and all were noble, riding horses to the palace gate in the morning. At Qujiang, they competed for bathing, and the lost jewels were not worth mentioning. At this time, the begonia was still not fully rested, and the hibiscus curtain was warm with fragrance. The beauties of the six palaces had no color, abandoning the beauties Jiang Caiping. Although ten bushels of pearls were personally bestowed, the door was deserted at night. Unexpectedly, Taizhen offended the king's anger, and the dedication of hair still touched the dragon's grace. Have you not heard that a rider brings fresh lychees from afar, but the common people are not as good as the beauty's heart. Just at the night of the Cowherd and Weaver Girl stars, they make oaths of life after life. Who knows that joy had not yet deepened when sorrow arrived. In a moment, the war drums of Yuyang stirred sorrow. It was all because of Lushan's rebellion, the disaster started from within the walls. Because there had been peace in the world for a long time, and the threat of war had been quelled, there were few ministers. What could be done? The king fled west, running for a long journey. Alas, a piece of light silk was tragic and ill-fated, and her fragrant soul fell under Mawei Slope. Fortunately, the smoke of war was extinguished and the royal carriage returned to the capital. I only see that the white-haired concubines are old, and half of the Pear Garden disciples have withered. Sad past events are looked back on in vain, death is far away and cannot be reborn. The sound of the bell in Jiange is about to break the soul, competing to see the silk stockings in the winery village. Later, I wanted to teach the sorcerers to seek them out, but the palace of Penglai was not real. What is the reason that the king is lost in a dream? The emotional sky and the sea of ​​hatred are unreal. If someone sings "Palace of Eternal Life", it will not be listened to as a normal song. Could it be that the rise and fall of governance is a reflection of the past and present?

Shen Bao Architecture Weekly

A Brief Discussion on Ancient Chinese Architecture (Part 1)

— Shi Dong

The development of Chinese architecture has a very long history. In this long process of development, the building materials used by the architectural community are mostly brick (甎), wood, stone, and mud. Among them, brick has long been widely used in various parts of China. According to various documents, the use of brick as a building material dates back to before the Zhou Dynasty; and its initial use was most prevalent in various parts of the Yellow River Basin. As for wood, it was mostly used in the Yangtze River Basin and southern regions. At that time, there were also buildings in various parts of the Yellow River Basin that mixed brick and wood. For example, the widespread distribution of houses mixing brick and wood in various parts of China can be cited as one of the examples. Stone was also used as a building material at that time, just like brick and wood. And the use of mud as a building material was most common in the northern parts of China in the past. Since the northern regions lacked wood and had little rainfall, mud was the most suitable material for the construction of houses. At this point, the Chinese architectural method was determined by the use of building materials; however, later, as a result of the development of the use of stone and brick, the structure of arches also developed very early, and the frame structure of domes also emerged one after another. Conversely, in this long period, pure wooden houses were not very developed. The architectural method in China since ancient times has focused entirely on the design and decoration of details, that is, focusing exclusively on the external appearance, so the construction of wooden houses was also affected and not very developed.

As for the front of Chinese buildings, the composition method that is uniformly symmetrical front and back, left and right, is usually adopted. For example, from palaces to temples, residences, and tombs, all adopt the composition method that is uniformly symmetrical front and back, left and right. This structural method can be said to be a congenital quirk of the Chinese people; and this idea is not only expressed in the building aspect, such as the arrangement method of stools in the room, and the love of couplets in articles, it can be said that this is the expression of this idea. Also, what is the characteristic of the appearance of ancient Chinese buildings? Its characteristics lie in the use of gorgeous colors, rich detailed designs, and special roofs. At the same time, painting colors on the exterior of buildings is also a characteristic of the Chinese people. For example, painting colors on wood, or using glazed tiles as the exterior of the wall are all examples. From this point, it can be known that color and Chinese buildings are indeed inseparable. However, there has always been a regulation on the use of colors since ancient times; that is, according to the theory of yin and yang and the five elements, the five colors of blue, red, white, yellow, and black are used, because these five colors are symbols of auspiciousness, and later, many very strong and stimulating colors were formulated based on these simple five colors. Also, the richness of the detailed design in Chinese buildings is truly the first in the world. Taking the shape of the window as an example, there are not only square, round, oval, and polygonal shapes; in addition, there are also pot-shaped, flat, arc-shaped, and grid-shaped shapes. And the changes in the window lattices are even more complex, with swastika series, polygonal series, ice-character series, text series, and carving series; it is not uncommon for the window lattice forms of buildings in a city to reach hundreds of kinds. As for the form of the roof, there are also fish-hanging shapes, column base shapes, tree-arch shapes, etc. The precision of its detailed craftsmanship is truly enough to amaze people. Furthermore, in terms of the form of the roof, the Chinese architectural method, for the external characteristics, that is, the structure of the roof, must be concave in principle. This roof shape is not common in the north, but most of the buildings in the south belong to this shape. The reason why the construction methods in the north and south differ from each other is also due to the different characteristics of the north and south ethnic groups. Furthermore, this is also enough to glimpse that paying attention to the special beauty of the appearance is also one of the elements of Chinese buildings.

Observing Some New Rules of the City's Stadium

— Ouyang Gu

Whether it's a venue for public gatherings or a sports stadium, both are important lifelines for training people to maintain order and to build physical fitness. Therefore, in Europe and America, such as Los Angeles in the United States and Versailles in France, great sports stadiums are built in the suburbs. However, the designs of such buildings are based on the principles of being grand, beautiful, and safe, as well as economical and practical. Thus, its position has become a special architectural art, which is very different from ordinary construction methods. Fortunately, the National Games, which caused a sensation throughout the country, has already concluded. This great building—the stadium—rarely seen in the city, provides us with a detailed observation. In this indelible great building, we can find the new rules about architecture that we need, many of which are indeed not commonly seen. The following brief notes, though less than one-tenth or one-twentieth, are small in words but show great meaning. The rest remains to be discovered, because the design of these new rules are all handled and supervised by Chinese people, without any foreign involvement. If it is promoted and applied in the future, who can say that it is not a good phenomenon in the Chinese architectural field!

Regarding the prevention of thermal expansion and contraction of cement pilasters, scientific and physical methods are applied as much as possible. At each cement section of the bleachers, a five-fen-or-so expansion joint is left between the adjacent sections to accommodate the expansion and contraction caused by external temperature changes. The cement and trass composition of these cement pilasters cannot be neglected, as they form the foundation of the bleachers. Therefore, the mixing ratio is based on a volume ratio of 1:2:4. The internal steel bars are also specified to have a tensile strength of 1,250 kilograms per square centimeter. Furthermore, one thing that can be used as a general reference is that, according to insiders, the method of inspecting the steel frame structure during construction was particularly novel, that is, no matter what kind of steel material is specified, the maximum tensile strength per square centimeter must not be less than 4,200 kilograms. When assembling, first refer to the roof plan, carefully note the size, and only after checking that there are no errors can the steel be cut and punched. All rivets are also tightly fastened. The method of inspection is to strike each one with a small hammer. Those that are tight will produce a crisp sound, while those that are loose will produce a broken, dull sound.

The lighting in the exercise hall and gym is purely high-angle. The periphery of the domed roof is fitted with frosted glass wire skylights, which can eliminate all dazzling bright light. Moreover, the gym floor is padded with oil felt, lined with pine tongue-and-groove boards, and covered with械木Marle, eliminating any possibility of radiant light and completely insulating against underground moisture, which can be considered very perfect. Furthermore, when the National Games began, the swimming competition was scheduled in the evening. The lighting equipment in the swimming pool was even more amazing. The lights were installed below the horizontal plane of the pool wall. During the competition, the lights and the water color were very harmonious. Presumably, when building, on the one hand, the installation of the glass cover of the pool wall was completely impermeable to water, and on the other hand, it was necessary to prevent leakage from the cement bends and joints. Unexpectedly, when applied today, it has such achievements. This can also be seen as a new path for the development of Chinese technology.

The podium and VIP reception area set up in the main hall of the venue have a steel frame canopy built above them, extending horizontally in the air. The excellence and strangeness of the design is rare even in the entire city of Shanghai. This cantilevered steel frame is about thirteen feet long, covered with a glass canopy, and suspended in the air on three sides without any support bars. It is indeed a strange design of the latest type. The current National Games opened for a total of ten days. At least one million people from China and abroad arrived to visit. Therefore, great efforts were also made for the external aesthetics of the stadium. We first observed the entire venue's building, and we did not find a single chimney. During construction, efforts were made to make the setting of chimneys elegant, so they were all hidden above the roof of the giant Ding-shaped gate tower. The towers still stand tall, so at first glance, who would think that they are the chimney pipes for setting up stoves! The red brick clear water walls, cement pillars, and large materials on the remaining four sides are all placed inside the wall and hidden from view, which is very neat and beautiful, and seems to be in line with the neat conditions of architecture.

Regarding the construction and construction situation and process of the remaining parts, this magazine's Double Ten Festival special issue on architecture has already said in great detail, so I don't want to go into too much detail here. We will now look at such a vast and great building. According to the value of the work and material cost report disclosed by the project management office there, the amount is also very low, because the materials used are mostly domestic products. Also, after looking at the table below, you will know its exact number:

Building construction 995,300

Sanitary equipment 69,000

Electrical equipment 17,300

Swimming pool water supply equipment 34,500

Ditches 7,800

Running track 6,700

Ball field 1,400

Lead wire steel 8,000

Cement road 7,000

Backfilling engineering 15,000

Wooden bleachers 6,000

Total 1,168,100 yuan

In addition, all engineering design and supervision matters of the stadium are planned and cooperated by various agencies in the city, without any foreign involvement. For all architectural materials, domestic products are used as much as possible, which shows that the authorities are sincerely promoting domestic products in the midst of efforts to build. This is worthy of emulation by the architectural community.

Swedish Public Housing Architecture

— Bu Ren

The Swedish public housing construction movement began in 1916, and the main organizer was the Stockholm Housing Cooperative. This cooperative was founded by the General Federation of Labor; the members of the cooperative are the future residents, and they are mostly low-income class. They have the opportunity to participate in the construction and management of the houses that serve as their residences. By 1922, the cooperative's plan had been largely realized, and it further engaged in a nationwide movement.

Under this movement, a group called "Savings Building Society" (Hyresgasternas SparkasseochByggnadsforening—referred to as H.B.S.) began to be established. The amazing achievements of public housing construction currently seen in Swedish cities must be attributed to this H.B.S and its chief architect, Sven Wallander.

The Savings Building Society, headquartered in Stockholm, is a rather complex organization. It buys land, or leases land for a long term. After the houses are built, the headquarters sells them to various residential branch offices. The headquarters records accounts, manages finances, sells houses, and purchases fuel and other supplies for branch offices. The entire organization is managed by a trust committee, whose members are publicly elected by representatives of the branch offices and re-elected annually.

Residents, i.e., those who buy houses, are members of the Savings Building Society. When a member joins the society, they should purchase one share, which costs 15 yuan, with an annual interest rate of 6%, and pay 10% to 15% of the house price. The remaining shortfall is paid by the headquarters, and this expense is mostly borrowed from the National Savings Bank and insurance companies.

Houses are divided into three types: A, B, and C. Therefore, members are also divided into three types: A, B, and C. The price of type A houses ranges from 2,000 yuan to more than 10,000 yuan, and the annual rent ranges from 150 yuan to more than 800 yuan. The price of type B houses ranges from 400 yuan to 2,000 yuan, and the annual rent ranges from 120 yuan to 500 yuan. Type C members do not pay the house price when joining the society, but only need to pay the rent annually.

Taking a type B member paying 200 yuan per year as an example, the use of the annual rent is as follows:

Loan interest... 120.00 yuan

Loan amortization... 35.00 yuan

Supply... 21.00 yuan

Heating and hot water... 16.00 yuan

Repair... 6.50 yuan

Reserve... 1.50 yuan

Total 200.00 yuan

After twenty years, the loan will be fully paid off, and the house will belong to the resident. However, the resident must still pay a considerable rent each year to cover repairs, supplies, and other expenses. Residents who have obtained ownership of the house can sell or rent the house, but must seek the consent of H·S·B·.

Architectural Jargon (19)

— Mei Zhenhuan

— Regarding use in the construction site —

Full Foot (滿脚)—If it is not in accordance with another term in the construction site, then the meaning of Full Foot (Fill Mud) is to fill the mud, because the progress of the work in the construction site takes a certain step, and Full Foot is after setting up the large footing (Footing) (note that setting up the large footing is also one of the jargons,) to speak further, Full Foot is the abbreviation of Filling the footing.

Turning Arrangement (翻排)—When bricklayers are building a wall, when their hands can't reach the height of the wall, they have to put up scaffolding (note that putting up scaffolding is also one of the jargons.) Scaffolding is divided into wood and bamboo. Wooden scaffolding can only be used for buildings with five or six floors. For ordinary two- or three-story houses, it is more common to use bamboo scaffolding, because the materials used for wooden scaffolding are complicated, such as rushing to the sky, top support, foot immersion, and air carrying, and the labor is also much more wasteful, so it is more economically cost-effective to use bamboo scaffolding. Now, when it comes to turning arrangement, what does it mean? That is when bricklayers are building a wall, when their hands can't reach the height of the wall, from the ground, they can only call it putting up scaffolding, but upwards they can't call it putting up scaffolding, they can only call it turning arrangement, which means turning the scaffolding board up one row.

Catching Sample (捉樣)—Regardless of the size of the project, in the organization of personnel, in addition to the supervisor, there is also the sample maker. Concerned, waiting to rule the lower-level doers, the sample maker (detailed before)'s job, as the name suggests, of course puts his mind on the drawings (called the blue sample in the construction site.) The meaning of catching sample is that the sample maker enlarges the dimensions on the blue sample, but in the construction site it is not called enlarging the sample but catching sample.

Blue Sample (藍樣子)—The blue sample itself is not blue, it only turns blue after a scientific action, in addition to the blue sample having its place in the construction site, there is also a consultation sample, that is, the sample approved by the Shanghai Municipal Council or the Public Works Bureau in the concession.
